    <script type="text/javascript">
    var AL2017SurveySectionComplete = false;
    var AL2017SurveyLetterStart = false;
    var AL2017TookSurvey = false;
    var AL2017TookSurvey2 = false;
    var SurveyLink = "";
    var SurveyHTMLB = 'http://web.gatesnotes.com/cn/aaaxh/sitesurvey';
    var SurveyHTMLA = 'http://opco.me/A19918B';
    var SurveyAPercentage = 50;
    var SurveyBPercentage = 50;
    var InitialPoolPercentage = 0;
    var SurveySpecialURLs = '{"URLS":{"ITEMS":[';
    var SurveySpecialURL = false;
    var SurveyALURL = false;
    var SurveyEnabled = true;
    // make JSON from special URLs
    $(function () {
        var lastChar = SurveySpecialURLs.substr(SurveySpecialURLs.length - 1);
        if (lastChar == ",") {
            // remove last comma
            SurveySpecialURLs = SurveySpecialURLs.slice(0, -1)
        }
        SurveySpecialURLs += ']}}';
    });
    $(document).ready(function () {
        // convert JSON to obj
        var Surveyobj = jQuery.parseJSON( SurveySpecialURLs );
        for (i = 0; i < Surveyobj.URLS.ITEMS.length; ++i) {
            // test to see if our page matches any of the special case URLs setup in sitecore
            if (Surveyobj.URLS.ITEMS[i].URL == window.location.pathname) {
                SurveySpecialURL = true;
                SurveyHTMLA = Surveyobj.URLS.ITEMS[i].A;
                SurveyHTMLB = Surveyobj.URLS.ITEMS[i].B;
                SurveyAPercentage = Surveyobj.URLS.ITEMS[i].APercentage;
                SurveyBPercentage = Surveyobj.URLS.ITEMS[i].BPercentage;
                InitialPoolPercentage = Surveyobj.URLS.ITEMS[i].InitialPoolPercentage;
                // special AL code
                if (Surveyobj.URLS.ITEMS[i].URL == "/2017-Annual-Letter") {
                    SurveyALURL = true;
                }
            }
        }
        SurveyAPercentage = parseInt(SurveyAPercentage);
        SurveyBPercentage = parseInt(SurveyBPercentage);
        InitialPoolPercentage = parseInt(InitialPoolPercentage);
        //console.log("SurveyAPercentage+SurveyBPercentage:"+(SurveyAPercentage+SurveyBPercentage));
        if ((SurveyAPercentage+SurveyBPercentage) == 0) {
            SurveyEnabled = false;
            console.log("Survey:disabled");
        }

        if (document.domain === 'www.gatesnotes.com') {
            // disabled so we can test on all domains
        }
        if (SurveyALURL) {
            // AL page
            if (!docCookies.hasItem('surveyedAL')) {
                if (filterUser()) {
                    if (SurveyEnabled) {
                        delayPopup();
                    }
                }
            } else {
                // renew cookie for frequent visitors
                setCookie("renew");
            }
        } else if (SurveySpecialURL) {
            // Special page
            if (!docCookies.hasItem('surveyedSP')) {
                if (filterUser()) {
                    if (SurveyEnabled) {
                        delayPopup();
                    }
                }
            } else {
                // renew cookie for frequent visitors
                setCookie("renew");
            }
        } else {
            // normal page
            // if user has taken any survey recently don't show them another, reset cookie
            if (!docCookies.hasItem('surveyed')) {
                if (filterUser()) {
                    if (SurveyEnabled) {
                        delayPopup();
                    }
                } else {
                    // keep user in pool
                }
            } else {
                // renew cookie for frequent visitors
                setCookie("renew");
            }
        }



        //manually trigger survey via Query String
        var surveyParam = s.getQueryParam('survey');
        if (surveyParam != "" && surveyParam != null) {
            if (surveyParam == "on") {
                showPopup();
            }
        }

    });

    function setCookie(reason) {
        console.log("Survey:"+reason);
        if (SurveyALURL) {
            console.log("surveyedAL");
            docCookies.setItem('surveyedAL', new Date().getTime(), 31536e3, '/', document.domain);
            docCookies.setItem('surveyed', new Date().getTime(), 31536e3, '/', document.domain);
        } else if (SurveySpecialURL) {
            console.log("surveyedSP");
            docCookies.setItem('surveyedSP', new Date().getTime(), 31536e3, '/', document.domain);
            docCookies.setItem('surveyed', new Date().getTime(), 31536e3, '/', document.domain);
        } else {
            console.log("surveyed");
            docCookies.setItem('surveyed', new Date().getTime(), 31536e3, '/', document.domain);
        }
    }

    function monitorComplete() {
        if (AL2017TookSurvey && AL2017SurveySectionComplete && !AL2017TookSurvey2) {
            AL2017TookSurvey2 = true;
            showPopup();
        }
    }

    function showPopup() {
        if (filterSurvey(SurveyAPercentage)) {
            // survey A
            SurveyLink = SurveyHTMLA;
        } else {
            // survey B
            SurveyLink = SurveyHTMLB;
        }
        surveyOn = true;
        $(".ALS_Holder").css("display", "none");
        $.colorbox({
            'href': '/TGN/surveyCD.html',
            'opacity': 0.6,
            'transition': 'none',
            'closeButton': false
        });
        setCookie("new");
    }
    function filterSurvey(P) {
        return Math.random() <= parseInt(P)/100;
    }
    function filterUser() {
        return Math.random() <= parseInt(InitialPoolPercentage)/100;
    }

    function getTime() {
        var valueStart, valueEnd, cookieStart = document.cookie.indexOf('surveyed');

        if (cookieStart == -1) {
            return '';
        } else {
            valueStart = document.cookie.indexOf('=', cookieStart) + 1;
            valueEnd = document.cookie.indexOf(';', cookieStart);

            if (valueEnd == -1) {
                valueEnd = document.cookie.length;
            }

            return document.cookie.substring(valueStart, valueEnd);
        }
    }

    function delayPopup(startTime) {
        var howLongToWait, now = new Date().getTime();

        startTime = parseInt(startTime);

        //if (startTime == NaN) {
        //    howLongToWait = 60000;
        //} else {
        //    howLongToWait = 60000 - (now - startTime);
        //}
        howLongToWait = 2000;

        setTimeout(showPopup, howLongToWait);
    }

    /*\
    |*|
    |*|  :: cookies.js ::
    |*|
    |*|  A complete cookies reader/writer framework with full unicode support.
    |*|
    |*|  https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/DOM/document.cookie
    |*|
    |*|  This framework is released under the GNU Public License, version 3 or later.
    |*|  http://www.gnu.org/licenses/gpl-3.0-standalone.html
    |*|
    |*|  Syntaxes:
    |*|
    |*|  * docCookies.setItem(name, value[, end[, path[, domain[, secure]]]])
    |*|  * docCookies.getItem(name)
    |*|  * docCookies.removeItem(name[, path])
    |*|  * docCookies.hasItem(name)
    |*|  * docCookies.keys()
    |*|
    \*/

    var docCookies = {
        getItem: function (sKey) {
            return unescape(document.cookie.replace(new RegExp("(?:(?:^|.*;)\\s*" + escape(sKey).replace(/[\-\.\+\*]/g, "\\$&") + "\\s*\\=\\s*([^;]*).*$)|^.*$"), "$1")) || null;
        },
        setItem: function (sKey, sValue, vEnd, sPath, sDomain, bSecure) {
            if (!sKey || /^(?:expires|max\-age|path|domain|secure)$/i.test(sKey)) { return false; }
            var sExpires = "";
            if (vEnd) {
                switch (vEnd.constructor) {
                    case Number:
                        sExpires = vEnd === Infinity ? "; expires=Fri, 31 Dec 9999 23:59:59 GMT" : "; max-age=" + vEnd;
                        break;
                    case String:
                        sExpires = "; expires=" + vEnd;
                        break;
                    case Date:
                        sExpires = "; expires=" + vEnd.toGMTString();
                        break;
                }
            }
            document.cookie = escape(sKey) + "=" + escape(sValue) + sExpires + (sDomain ? "; domain=" + sDomain : "") + (sPath ? "; path=" + sPath : "") + (bSecure ? "; secure" : "");
            return true;
        },
        removeItem: function (sKey, sPath) {
            if (!sKey || !this.hasItem(sKey)) { return false; }
            document.cookie = escape(sKey) + "=; expires=Thu, 01 Jan 1970 00:00:00 GMT" + (sPath ? "; path=" + sPath : "");
            return true;
        },
        hasItem: function (sKey) {
            return (new RegExp("(?:^|;\\s*)" + escape(sKey).replace(/[\-\.\+\*]/g, "\\$&") + "\\s*\\=")).test(document.cookie);
        },
        keys: function () { /* optional method: you can safely remove it! */
            var aKeys = document.cookie.replace(/((?:^|\s*;)[^\=]+)(?=;|$)|^\s*|\s*(?:\=[^;]*)?(?:\1|$)/g, "").split(/\s*(?:\=[^;]*)?;\s*/);
            for (var nIdx = 0; nIdx < aKeys.length; nIdx++) { aKeys[nIdx] = unescape(aKeys[nIdx]); }
            return aKeys;
        }
    };
</script>
<script type="text/javascript">
    //var GIURL = "https://gnquiz-staging.azurewebsites.net/api/Account/";
    var GIURL = "https://insiders.gatesnotes.com/api/Account/";
    var ItemStoreLookDataPoints = [];
    var ItemStoreLookDataPrize = [];
    var TGNARR_CampaignUserPrizes = [];
    var TGNARR_CampaignUserPrizesEarned = [];

    function setGI(group, item, type, value, user, st) {
        $.ajax({
            url: GIURL + "GIStore",
            dataType: "json",
            type: "POST",
            headers: { 'authorization': 'Bearer ' + localStorage.getItem(tokenKey) },
            data: {
                //GNIName: "",//user, // this is for testing only
                Group: group,
                Item: item,
                Type: type,
                Value: value,
                StorageType: st // 0 WriteOnce, 1 WriteMany, 2 WriteLast
            },
            success: function (data) {
                console.log("OK" + data);
            },
            error: function (request, status, error) {
                console.log("ERROR:" + request.responseText);
            }
        });
    }

    function lookGI(groups, item, types, user) {
        $.ajax({
            url: GIURL + "GILook",
            dataType: "json",
            headers: { 'authorization': 'Bearer ' + localStorage.getItem(tokenKey) },
            type: "POST",
            data: {
                //GNIName: "",//user, // for test
                GroupsCSV: groups,
                TypesCSV: types,
                Item: item,
            },
            success: function (data) {
                //console.log("OK" + data);
                if (types == "Points") {
                    ItemStoreLookDataPoints = data;
                }
                if (types == "Prize") {
                    ItemStoreLookDataPrize = data;
                    try {
                        // add to Prize list
                        if ($.inArray(data[0].Group, TGNARR_CampaignUserPrizes) == -1) {
                            TGNARR_CampaignUserPrizes.push(data[0].Group);
                        }
                        // add to list of earned prizes
                        if ($.inArray(data[0].Item, TGNARR_CampaignUserPrizesEarned) == -1 && data[0].Value == 1) {
                            TGNARR_CampaignUserPrizesEarned.push(data[0].Item);
                        }
                        //console.log("GIPrize:Item:" + data[0].Item + ":Value:" + data[0].Value + ":InEarned:" + $.inArray(data[0].Item, TGNARR_CampaignUserPrizesEarned));
                    } catch (error) {
                    }
                }
            },
            error: function (request, status, error) {
                console.log("ERROR:" + request.responseText);
            }
        });
    }

    function lookGICount(group, item) {
        $.ajax({
            url: GIURL + "GICount",
            dataType: "json",
            type: "POST",
            data: {
                Group: group,
                Item: item,
            },
            success: function (data) {
                //console.log("OK" + data);
            },
            error: function (request, status, error) {
                console.log("ERROR:" + request.responseText);
            }
        });
    }

    function setCRMField(field, value, type) {//type="string", "Yes/No", "integer"//fields:new_gaveaflock
        $.ajax({
            url: GIURL + "CRMFieldSet",
            dataType: "json",
            headers: { 'authorization': 'Bearer ' + localStorage.getItem(tokenKey) },
            type: "POST",
            data: {
                field: field,
                value: value,
                fieldType: type,
            },
            success: function (data) {
                console.log("OK" + data);
            },
            error: function (request, status, error) {
                console.log("ERROR:" + request.responseText);
            }
        });
    }
    
</script>

    function mobart_SetUserGNI() {
        $("#mobart_Art_SI_block").css("display", "none");
        $("#mobart_Art_USER_block").css("display", "block");

    function mobart_SetUserNONE() {
        location.reload();

    $(document).ready(function () {

        //Hook up sharing urls from Sharewidget
        console.log("banner DocReady");
        $(".socbannershareiconFBa").attr("href", $(".widgetbody").find(".fbShareClick").attr('href'));
        $(".socbannershareiconTWa").attr("href", $(".widgetbody").find(".twShareClick").attr('href'));
        $(".socbannershareiconFBa").attr("onclick", $(".widgetbody").find(".fbShareClick").attr('onclick'));
        $(".socbannershareiconTWa").attr("onclick", $(".widgetbody").find(".twShareClick").attr('onclick'));
        $(".socbannershareiconEMa").attr("href", $(".widgetbody").find(".emShare").attr('href'));
        $(".socbannershareiconEMa").attr("onclick", $(".widgetbody").find(".emShare").attr('onclick'));

        $(".mobartshareiconFBa").attr("href", $(".widgetbody").find(".fbShareClick").attr('href'));
        $(".mobartshareiconTWa").attr("href", $(".widgetbody").find(".twShareClick").attr('href'));
        $(".mobartshareiconFBa").attr("onclick", $(".widgetbody").find(".fbShareClick").attr('onclick'));
        $(".mobartshareiconTWa").attr("onclick", $(".widgetbody").find(".twShareClick").attr('onclick'));
        $(".mobartshareiconEMa").attr("href", $(".widgetbody").find(".emShare").attr('href'));
        $(".mobartshareiconEMa").attr("onclick", $(".widgetbody").find(".emShare").attr('onclick'));

        $(".mobartshareiconFBa").click(function () {
            s.eVar9 = "facebook";
            s.eVar14 = document.title;
            doOmnitureEvent("event11");
        });
        $(".mobartshareiconTWa").click(function () {
            s.eVar9 = "twitter";
            s.eVar14 = document.title;
            doOmnitureEvent("event11");
        });
        $(".mobartshareiconEMa").click(function () {
            s.eVar9 = "email";
            s.eVar14 = document.title;
            doOmnitureEvent("event11");
        });
        function doOmnitureEvent(event) {
            try {
                s.linkTrackVars = "events,eVar9,eVar14";
                s.linkTrackEvents = "event11";
                s.events = event;
                s.tl(true, 'o', 'article');
            } catch (e) {
                console.log(e.message);
                console.log(e.name);
            }
        }

        
        $(".banartshare").click(function (event) {
            if ($(".banartshare i").hasClass("icon-share_5")) {
                $(".banartshare i").removeClass("icon-share_5");
                $(".banartshare i").addClass("icon-close_thin");
                $(".banartheadline").hide();
                $("#artgosocov2").show();
            }
            else {
                $(".banartshare i").removeClass("icon-close_thin");
                $(".banartshare i").addClass("icon-share_5");
                $("#artgosocov2").hide();
                $(".banartheadline").show();
            }
        });

        // Mac Chrome fix
        //if (navigator.userAgent.indexOf('Mac OS X') != -1) {
        //    // mac
        //} else {
        //    // pc
        //}
        //(function ($) {
        //    // console.log(navigator.userAgent);
        //    /* Adjustments for Safari on Mac */

        //        // console.log('Safari on Mac detected, applying class...');
        //        $('html').addClass('safari-mac'); // provide a class for the safari-mac specific css to filter with
        //    }
        //})(jQuery);

 //* to take into account different font metrics */
 //       .safari-mac #page4 .section p.fussyDesigner { margin-right: -15px; }
 //       .safari-mac #page8 .section-footer { width: 694px; }
        
        var updateBannerSize = function () {
            var ww = $(window).width();
            var wh = $(window).height();
            if (ww < 380) {
                $(".bannermobmenu i").removeClass("icon-list");
                $(".bannermobmenu i").addClass("icon-list_08");
            } else {
                $(".bannermobmenu i").removeClass("icon-list_08");
                $(".bannermobmenu i").addClass("icon-list");
            }
        };
        // turn back on for gatesBurger

    //params

    var GetRolloverDate = function (datestring) {
        var d = $.datepicker.parseDate("MM dd, yy", datestring);
        var Today = new Date();
        var dayCount = Calculatedays(d, Today);
        var myRollOverDate = CalculateRollOverDate(dayCount);
        return myRollOverDate;
    }
    var Calculatedays = function (date1, date2) {

        //Get 1 day in milliseconds
        var one_day = 1000 * 60 * 60 * 24;

        // Convert both dates to milliseconds
        var date1_ms = date1.getTime();
        var date2_ms = date2.getTime();

        // Calculate the difference in milliseconds
        var difference_ms = date2_ms - date1_ms;

        // Convert back to days and return
        var days = Math.floor(difference_ms / one_day);
        return days;
    };
    var CalculateRollOverDate = function (days) {

        var months = Math.floor(days / 30);
        var years = Math.floor(days / 365);
        if (days <= 0) {
            return "Posted today";
        }
        else if (days == 1) {
            return "Posted yesterday";
        }
        else if (days <= 30) {
            return "Posted " + days + " days ago";
        }
        else if (months < 2) {
            return "Posted " + months + " month ago";
        }
        else if (months < 13) {
            return "Posted " + months + " months ago";
        }
        else if (years < 2) {
            return "Posted " + years + " year ago";
        }
        else {
            return "Posted " + years + " years ago";
        }
    };

    }

    function addNewYears() {

    // TIMER
    var SPthat = null;
    var SPtime = null;
    var SPtimer = null;
    var mySearchPageTimer = function () {
        SPthat = this,
            SPtime = timeVal,
            SPtimer;
        SPthat.set = function () {
            //console.log('setting up timer');
            SPtimer = setInterval(function () {
                //console.log('running time: ' + SPtime);
                SPtime--;
                if (SPtime < 0) {
                    mySearchPageTimer.reset();
                    mySearchPageTimer.set();
                    SPtime = timeVal;
                    tosinput();
                }
                if (SPtime == 4) {
                    // trigger fade out animation .tosResultsBox opacity to 0
                    var searchBox = $("#tosinput");
                    searchTerm = searchBox.val();
                    //console.log("ST: "+searchTerm+" STW: "+searchTermWas)
                    // && searchTerm !== $('#tosinput').attr('placeholder') && searchTerm !== ""
                    if (searchTerm !== searchTermWas && searchTerm != "") {
                        fadeOutResults();
                    }
                }
            }, 100);
        }
        SPthat.reset = function () {
            //console.log('clearing timer');
            SPtime = timeVal;
            clearInterval(SPtimer);
        }
        return SPthat;
    }();

    function searchFromURL() {
        // Get search string from url and set the value of the 'your search' box to that
        if (document.location.search !== undefined) {
            if ((document.location.pathname.toLowerCase() == "/search") || (document.location.pathname.toLowerCase() == "/globalpages/searchx")) {
                if (document.location.search.indexOf('=') !== -1) {
                    var queryIndex = document.location.search.indexOf('=') + 1;
                    var searchString = document.location.search.substring(queryIndex);
                    if (searchString.length > 0) {
                        $("#searchResultsBox2").val(decodeURI(searchString));
                        $("#searchResultsBox3").val(decodeURI(searchString));
                        $("#Text1").val(decodeURI(searchString));
                        $("#tosinput").val(decodeURI(searchString));

                    }
                } else {
                    $("#tosinput").val("");
                }
                tosinput();
                //opensearch();

                if ($("#tosearch").hasClass("open")) {
                } else {
                    $(".AH_Holder").css("display", "none");
                    $("#tosearch").addClass("open");
                    if (document.location.pathname.toLowerCase() === "/all" || window.location.pathname.toLowerCase() === "/all") {

                    } else {
                        $(".SearchheroHolder").css("display", "none");
                    }

                }

                //$(".footerh").css("display", "none");
            }
        }
    }

    // Get Top Results for a specified SEARCH TERM
    function GetSearchResultTopResultArticleSet(validYearsString, searchTerm) {
        // JSON
        $.ajax({
            url: "/tgnservices/BlogRollService.asmx/GetSearchResultTopResultArticleSet?validYearsString=" + validYearsString + "&searchTerm=" + searchTerm + "",
            dataType: "json",
            type: "GET",
            success: function (data) {
                var source = $("#searchTopResultTemplate").html();
                var template = Handlebars.compile(source);
                var html = template(data);
                var resultsReturnBox = $(".tosResultsBox");
                resultsReturnBox.prepend(html);
                resultsReturnBox.find(".TGN_RectBR_s5image").each(function (i, obj) {
                    if (i % 2 === 0) {
                        /* we are even */
                        $(this).parent().parent().attr("class", "TGN_RectBR_s5a");
                    }
                    else {
                        /* we are odd */
                        $(this).parent().parent().attr("class", "TGN_RectBR_s5b");
                    }
                });
                totalSearchResults += data.ArticleList.length;
                doOmniture("TopResults");
                topReturns = data.ArticleList.length;
                if (data.ArticleList.length > 0) {
                    RAPsubject = data.ArticleList[0].PreHeadline;
                }


                
                //console.log(data);
                //console.log("GetSearchResultTopResultArticleSet - " + "YEARS:" + validYearsString + " | " + "TERM:" + searchTerm + " | " + "DATA:" + data);
            },
            error: function (textStatus, errorThrown) {
                console.log("GetSearchResultTopResultArticleSet - " + "ERROR");
            }
        });
    }

    // Get a particular set of articles from the blogroll within specified years - Matching a specified SEARCH TERM
    function GetSearchResultArticleSet(validYearsString, setNumber, searchTerm, sortByType, sortByVideo) {
        $.ajax({
            url: "/tgnservices/BlogRollService.asmx/GetSearchResultArticleSet?validYearsString=" + validYearsString + "&setNumber=" + setNumber + "&searchTerm=" + searchTerm + "&sortByType=" + sortByType + "&sortByVideo=" + sortByVideo + "",
            dataType: "json",
            type: "GET",
            success: function (data) {
                var source = $("#searchResultTemplate").html();
                var template = Handlebars.compile(source);
                var html = template(data);
                var resultsReturnBox = $(".tosResultsBox");
                //resultsReturnBox.html(html);
                //resultsReturnBox.html(resultsReturnBox.html() + html);
                //
                // Change from append to insert in the correct possition in stream
                if (setNumber == "0") {
                    resultsReturnBox.append(html);
                } else {
                    var insertPositionNumber = 0;
                    if (totalSearchResults % 2 === 0) {
                        // no top result
                        insertPositionNumber = (setNumber * 10);
                    } else {
                        insertPositionNumber = ((setNumber * 10) + 1);
                    }
                    //console.log(resultsReturnBox.find('.otherSearchResults:nth-child(' + insertPositionNumber + ')').length);
                    if (resultsReturnBox.find('.otherSearchResults:nth-child(' + insertPositionNumber + ')').length) {
                        resultsReturnBox.find('.otherSearchResults:nth-child(' + insertPositionNumber + ')').after(html);
                    } else {
                        resultsReturnBox.append(html);
                    }
                }
                //resultsReturnBox.append(html);
                resultsReturnBox.find(".TGN_RectBR_s5image").each(function (i, obj) {
                    if (i % 2 === 0) {
                        /* we are even */
                        $(this).parent().parent().attr("class", "TGN_RectBR_s5a");
                    }
                    else {
                        /* we are odd */
                        $(this).parent().parent().attr("class", "TGN_RectBR_s5b");
                    }
                });
                //
                totalSearchResults += data.ArticleList.length;
                otherReturns = data.ArticleList.length;

                if (setNumber == 0 && otherReturns == 0) {
                    $("#noResultsPanel").css("display", "block");
                    if (topReturns > 0) {
                        $(".RAPanel").css("display", "block");
                        $(".RAPsubject").html(RAPsubject.toUpperCase());
                    } else {
                        $(".RAPanel").css("display", "none");
                    }
                    
                    //console.log($("#S_CK_ALL").parent().find('a').hasClass("filterOn") + curSortType);
                    if (!$("#S_CK_ALL").parent().find('a').hasClass("filterOn") || curSortType !== "all") {
                        $(".ifFiltersOn").css("display", "inline");
                    }else{
                        $(".ifFiltersOn").css("display", "none");
                    }
                } else {
                    $("#noResultsPanel").css("display", "none");
                    $(".RAPanel").css("display", "none");
                }
                doOmniture("SearchResults");
                //console.log(data.ArticleList.length);
                //console.log("GetBlogRollArticleSet - " + "HTML:" + html + "source:" + source + "template:" + template);
                //console.log("GetBlogRollArticleSet - " + "DATA:" + data);
                //console.log("GetSearchResultArticleSet - " + "SET:" + setNumber + " | " + "TERM:" + setNumber + " | " + "TYPE:" + setNumber + " | " + "DATA:" + data);
                //checkMobileView();
                setTimeout(function () {
                    setSearchHero();
                }, 150);
            }
        });
    }

    function getSetBRArticles(validYearsString, setNumber, sortByVideo) {

                    resultsReturnBox.html(html);
                } else {
                    //resultsReturnBox.html(resultsReturnBox.html() + html);
                    //

                        // no top result

                    } else {
                        insertPositionNumber = ((setNumber * 10) + 1);
                    }
                    //console.log(resultsReturnBox.find('.otherSearchResults:nth-child(' + insertPositionNumber + ')').length);
                    //resultsReturnBox.find('.otherSearchResults:nth-child(' + insertPositionNumber + ')').after(html);
                    if (resultsReturnBox.find('.otherSearchResults:nth-child(' + insertPositionNumber + ')').length) {
                        resultsReturnBox.find('.otherSearchResults:nth-child(' + insertPositionNumber + ')').after(html);
                    } else {
                        resultsReturnBox.append(html);
                    }
                    //resultsReturnBox.append(html);
                    // otherSearchResults
                }
                resultsReturnBox.find(".TGN_RectBR_s5image").each(function (i, obj) {
                    if (i % 2 === 0) {
                        /* we are even */
                        $(this).parent().parent().attr("class", "TGN_RectBR_s5a");
                    }
                    else {
                        /* we are odd */
                        $(this).parent().parent().attr("class", "TGN_RectBR_s5b");
                    }
                });
                $("#noResultsPanel").css("display", "none");
                $(".RAPanel").css("display", "none");
                doOmniture("BlogRollResults");
                totalSearchResults += data.ArticleList.length;
                topReturns = data.ArticleList.length;
                //console.log(data);

                //console.log("GetBlogRollArticleSet - " + "HTML:" + html + "source:" + source + "template:" + template);
                //console.log("GetBlogRollArticleSet - " + "DATA:" + data);
                //checkMobileView();
                setTimeout(function () {
                    setSearchHero();
                }, 150);
            }
        });
    }

    function resultssortTime(timeFrame, el) {
        if ($(el).find('a').text() == "All") {
            jQuery('.scb_blue').each(function () {
                $(this).css('background', 'white');
                $(this).parent().parent().find('a').removeClass("filterOn");
            });
            $(el).find('.SEARCHcheckbox').children(":first").css('background', '#3379be');
            $(el).find('a').addClass("filterOn");
        } else {

            $("#S_CK_ALL").children(":first").css('background', 'white');
            $("#S_CK_ALL").parent().find('a').removeClass("filterOn");
            if ($(el).find('a').hasClass("filterOn")) {
                $(el).find('a').removeClass("filterOn");
                $(el).find('.SEARCHcheckbox').children(":first").css('background', 'white');
            } else {
                $(el).find('a').addClass("filterOn");
                $(el).find('.SEARCHcheckbox').children(":first").css('background', '#3379be');
            }

        }
        validYearsString = "1920";
        var numberSelected = 0;
        jQuery('.restime').each(function () {
            if ($(this).hasClass("filterOn")) {
                numberSelected++;
            }
        });
        //console.log("numberSelected:" + numberSelected);
        if (numberSelected == 0) {
            $("#S_CK_ALL").children(":first").css('background', '#3379be');
            $("#S_CK_ALL").parent().find('a').addClass("filterOn");
        }
        jQuery('a.restime.filterOn').each(function () {
            if ($(this).hasClass("filterOn")) {
                if ($(this).html() == "All") {
                    validYearsString = "2020,2019,2018,2017,2016,2015,2014,2013,2012,2011,2010,2009";
                } else {
                    if ($(this).html() == "2010") {
                        validYearsString = $(this).html() + ",2009," + validYearsString;
                    } else {
                        validYearsString = $(this).html() + "," + validYearsString;
                    }
                }
            }
        });
        //console.log("VYS "+validYearsString);
        searchTermWas = "hcumgnihton";
        setNumber = 0;
    }

<script type="text/javascript">
    var currentShowing = 10;
    var initialResults = 10;
    var BR_ImageRatio = 800 / 493;

    function putMAG() {
        var TIWidth = $("#tosinput").width();
        $(".SPright").css("left", TIWidth + 0 + "px");
    }

    //set an interval
    setInterval(putMAG, 100);

    function setSearchHero() {
        //console.log(document.location.pathname.toLowerCase());
        if (document.location.pathname.toLowerCase() === "/all" || window.location.pathname.toLowerCase() === "/all" || document.location.pathname.toLowerCase() === "/search" || window.location.pathname.toLowerCase() === "/search" || document.location.pathname.toLowerCase() === "/books" || window.location.pathname.toLowerCase() === "/books") {
            //console.log("setSearchHero");
            var nh = 564;
            var ww = $(window).width();
            if (ww < 980) {
                $(".tosinput").css("width", ww - 130 + "px");
                if (ww < 500) {
                    nh = 500 * (564 / 1200);
                    $(".searchherohero").css("height", "235px");
                    $(".SearchheroHolder").css("height", "235px");
                }
                else {
                    nh = 720 * (564 / 1200);
                    $(".searchherohero").css("height", "376px");
                    $(".SearchheroHolder").css("height", "376px");
                }
                if (ww > 680) {
                    $(".TGN_RectBR_s5a").css("float", "left");
                    $(".TGN_RectBR_s5a").css("margin-right", "10px");
                    $(".TGN_RectBR_s5a").css("clear", "both");
                    $(".TGN_RectBR_s5b").css("float", "right");
                    $(".TGN_RectBR_s5b").css("margin-right", "0px");
                    $(".TGN_RectBR_s5a").css("width", +(ww - 90) / 2 + "px");
                    $(".TGN_RectBR_s5b").css("width", +(ww - 90) / 2 + "px");
                    $(".TGN_RectBR_s5image").css("height", +($(".TGN_RectBR_s5a").width() / BR_ImageRatio) + "px");
                } else {
                    $(".TGN_RectBR_s5a").css("float", "none");
                    $(".TGN_RectBR_s5a").css("margin-right", "0px");
                    $(".TGN_RectBR_s5a").css("width", "100%");
                    $(".TGN_RectBR_s5b").css("float", "none");
                    $(".TGN_RectBR_s5b").css("margin-right", "0px");
                    $(".TGN_RectBR_s5b").css("width", "100%");
                    $(".TGN_RectBR_s5image").css("height", +((ww - 50) / BR_ImageRatio) + "px");
                }
            } else {
                $(".tosinput").css("width", "70%");
                $(".searchherohero").css("height", "564px");
                $(".SearchheroHolder").css("height", "564px");
            }
            if ($(".tosearch").is(':visible')) {
                //$(".tosinput").focus();
                //console.log($('#tosinput').attr('placeholder'));
                if ($('#tosinput').val() == $('#tosinput').attr('placeholder')) {
                    //$('#tosinput').selectRange(0); // set cursor position at start
                } else {
                    var TIV = $('#tosinput').val();
                    //$('#tosinput').selectRange(TIV.length); // set cursor position at end
                }
            }

            checkMobileView();
        }
        setTimeout(function () {
            SearchAndBooksItemViewable();
        }, 150);

    }
    $.fn.selectRange = function (start, end) {
        //console.log("SR FUNC" + start);
        var searchBox = $("#tosinput");
        searchTerm = searchBox.val();
        if (searchTerm !== $('#tosinput').attr('placeholder')) {
            if (!end) end = start;
            return this.each(function () {
                if (this.setSelectionRange) {
                    this.focus();
                    this.setSelectionRange(start, end);
                } else if (this.createTextRange) {
                    var range = this.createTextRange();
                    range.collapse(true);
                    range.moveEnd('character', end);
                    range.moveStart('character', start);
                    range.select();
                }
            });
        }

    };

    $(window).load(function () {
        //checkMobileView();
        //console.log("runningSearchJS-WL");
        var getbackgroundimage = function (c, ctx) {
            var bg = c.css('background-image');
            bg = bg.replace('url(', '').replace(')', '').replace('"', '').replace('"', '');

            var imageObj = new Image();
            var width = ctx.canvas.width;
            var height = ctx.canvas.height;

            imageObj.onload = function () {
                var imagew = imageObj.width;
                var imageh = imageObj.height;
                var imagesw = width;
                var imagesh = height;
                var imagesx = (imagew - width) / 2;
                if (imagesx < 0) {
                    imagesx = 0;
                    imagesw = imagew;
                }
                var imagesy = (imageh - height) / 2;
                if (imagesy < 0) {
                    imagesy = 0;
                    imagesh = imageh;
                }
                ctx.drawImage(imageObj,
                    imagesx,
                    imagesy,
                    imagesw,
                    imagesh,
                    0,
                    0,
                    width,
                    height
                );
            };
            imageObj.src = bg;
        };

        var brightness = function (pixels, adjustment) {
            var d = pixels.data;
            for (var i = 0; i < d.length; i += 4) {
                d[i] += adjustment;
                d[i + 1] += adjustment;
                d[i + 2] += adjustment;
            }
            return pixels;
        };

        var ColorTint = function (pixels, r, g, b) {
            var d = pixels.data;
            for (var i = 0; i < d.length; i += 4) {
                d[i] += r;
                d[i + 1] += g;
                d[i + 2] += b;
                if (d[i] > 130) { d[i] += 2; } else { d[i] -= 10; }
                if (d[i + 1] > 130) { d[i + 1] += 2; } else { d[i + 1] -= 10; }
                if (d[i + 2] > 130) { d[i + 2] += 2; } else { d[i + 2] -= 10; }
            }
            return pixels;
        };

        IS_IPAD = navigator.userAgent.match(/iPad/i) != null;
        IS_IPHONE = (navigator.userAgent.match(/iPhone/i) != null) || (navigator.userAgent.match(/iPod/i) != null);
        if (IS_IPAD) {
            IS_IPHONE = false;

        $(document.body).on("mouseenter", ".SEARCHunit", function () {

            var RollOverDate = GetRolloverDate($(this).find(".TGN_RectBR_D_imageDATEtext").attr("data-dateval"));
            $(this).find(".TGN_RectBR_D_imageDATEtext").html(RollOverDate);

            var ww = $(window).width();
            if (ww > 680) {
                var ctx = $(this).find(".searchresultsthumb").get(0).getContext("2d");
                var width = ctx.canvas.width;
                var height = ctx.canvas.height;
                var width2 = $(this).find(".searchresultsthumb").width();
                var height2 = $(this).find(".searchresultsthumb").height();
                var pixels = ctx.getImageData(0, 0, width, height);
                ctx.putImageData(pixels, 0, 0);
                outerRadius = Math.sqrt(Math.pow(width / 2, 2) + Math.pow(height / 2, 2));
                ctx.globalCompositeOperation = 'source-over';
                gradient = ctx.createRadialGradient(width / 2, height / 2, 0, width / 2, height / 2, outerRadius);
                gradient.addColorStop(0, 'rgba(0,0,0,.65)');
                gradient.addColorStop(1, 'rgba(0,0,0,.65)');
                ctx.fillStyle = gradient;
                ctx.fillRect(0, 0, width, height);
                //
                $(this).find(".TGN_RectBR_D_imageDATE").css("display", "block");
                $(this).find(".TGN_RectBR_D_imageCTA").css("display", "block");
            }
            $(this).find(".hpheadline").css("text-decoration", "underline");
        });
        $(document.body).on("mouseleave", ".SEARCHunit", function () {
            //
            var ctx = $(this).find(".searchresultsthumb").get(0).getContext("2d");
            var width = ctx.canvas.width;
            var height = ctx.canvas.height;
            var img = new Image();
            img.src = "";
            ctx.save();
            ctx.setTransform(1, 0, 0, 1, 0, 0);
            ctx.clearRect(0, 0, width, height);
            ctx.restore();
            img.onload = function () {
                ctx.drawImage(img, 0, 0);
            };
            $(this).find(".TGN_RectBR_D_imageDATE").css("display", "none");
            $(this).find(".TGN_RectBR_D_imageCTA").css("display", "none");

    var checkMobileView = function () {
        var ww = $(window).width();

        if (ww <= 980) {

            $(".SEARCHshelf").css("display", "none");

            $(".searchTileContainer").css("max-width", "100%");
            $(".searchTileContainer").css("width", "100%");
            $(".otherSearchResults").css("display", "block");
        } else {
            //tile
            $(".searchlist").css("display", "none");
            $(".searchtile").css("display", "inline-block");
            $(".SEARCHshelf").css("display", "block");
            $(".searchTileContainer").css("left", "236px");
            //$(".searchTileContainer").css("max-width", newWidth + "px");
            $(".searchTileContainer").css("max-width", 980 + "px");
            $(".searchTileContainer").css("width", newWidth + "px");
            $(".SEARCHcolHead_Right").css("width", "934px");
            if (newWidth < 954) {
                $(".SEARCHcolHead_Right").css("width", "694px");
            }
            if (newWidth < 715) {
                $(".SEARCHcolHead_Right").css("width", "452px");
            }
            $(".otherSearchResults").css("display", "inline-block");
        }

        // hide book items for aritcle and vice versa
        jQuery('.hpSearchImageBook').each(function () {
            //console.log("SRC Length: " + $(this).attr('src').length);
            if ($(this).parent().attr("data-url").length < 2 && $(this).parent().attr("data-url") != "book") {
                $(this).parent().parent().css('display', 'none');

                $(this).parent().parent().parent().find('#content_0_searchResultsRepeater_imageThumb_1').css('display', 'none');

            //}
        });


    }
    function TGNSearchLoadVisibleThumbs() {
        jQuery('.hpSearchImageBook').each(function () {
            var attr = $(this).parent().attr("data-url");
            if (typeof attr !== typeof undefined && attr !== false) {
                // Search Result
                if ($(this).parent().parent().parent().is(':visible') && TGNSearchResultisOnScreen($(this))) {
                    if ($(this).parent().attr("data-url") != "set" && $(this).parent().attr("data-url") != "book") {
                        $(this).attr('src', $(this).parent().attr("data-url"));
                        if ($(this).parent().attr("data-url").length < 2) {
                            $(this).parent().attr("data-url", "set");
                        } else {
                            $(this).parent().attr("data-url", "book");
                        }
                    }
                    if ($(this).parent().parent().parent().find('.searchresultsthumb').attr("data-url") != "set") {
                        $(this).parent().parent().parent().find('.searchresultsthumb').css("background-image", "url('" + $(this).parent().parent().parent().find('.searchresultsthumb').attr("data-url") + "')");
                        $(this).parent().parent().parent().find('.searchresultsthumb').attr("data-url", "set");
                    }
                }
            }
        });

    function TGNSearchResultisOnScreen(element) {
        var curPos = element.offset();
        var curTop = curPos.top;
        var screenHeight = $(window).height();
        return (curTop > screenHeight) ? false : true;
    }
    var SPfirstTime = true;
    var tosinput = function () {

        var searchBox = $("#tosinput");
        searchTerm = searchBox.val();
        var searchTermClean = searchTerm.replace(/\#/g, '');
        if (searchTerm !== "" && searchTerm !== null && searchTerm !== $('#tosinput').attr('placeholder')) {
            if (searchTerm !== searchTermWas) {
                // load results for new search term
                if (SPfirstTime == true) {
                    SPfirstTime = false;
                } else {
                    var a = location.pathname;
                    window.history.pushState("", "", a + "?search=" + searchTerm);
                }
                totalSearchResults = 0;
                setNumber = 0; //noResultsTermBox
                searchScrollY = 0;
                var resultsReturnBox = $(".tosResultsBox");
                resultsReturnBox.html("");
                GetSearchResultTopResultArticleSet(validYearsString, searchTermClean);
                GetSearchResultArticleSet(validYearsString, 0, searchTermClean, sortByType, sortByVideo);
                searchTermWas = searchTerm;
            }
        } else {
            if (searchTerm !== searchTermWas) {
                setNumber = 0;
            }
            if (setNumber == 0 && $("#tosearch").hasClass("open") && searchTerm !== searchTermWas) {
                // get blogroll results
                if (SPfirstTime == true) {
                    SPfirstTime = false;
                }
                totalSearchResults = 0;
                //console.log("From tosinput");
                //console.log(setNumber + "," + totalSearchResults + "," + searchTerm + "," + searchTermWas);
                var resultsReturnBox = $(".tosResultsBox");
                resultsReturnBox.html("");
                getSetBRArticles(validYearsString, setNumber, sortByVideo);
                searchTermWas = searchTerm;
                //setNumber++;
            }
        }
        //console.log(setNumber + "," + totalSearchResults + "," + searchTerm);
        if (searchTerm !== $('#tosinput').attr('placeholder') && searchTerm !== "" || setNumber == 0) {
            fadeInResults();
            //checkMobileView();
        }
        $("#searchResultsFor").text("FOR \"" + searchTerm + "\"");
        $("#noResultsTermBox").text(searchTerm);
        $("#noFilterTermBox").text(searchTerm);
    };



    //Omniture stuff

    function doOmnitureEvent(event) {
        try {
            s.events = event
            s.linkTrackVars = 'events,eVar1,prop3,prop4';
            s.linkTrackEvents = event;
            s.tl(true, 'o', 'search');
            //console.log(event);
        } catch (e) {
            console.log(event);
            console.log(e.message);
            console.log(e.name);
        }
    }

    function doOmniture(SearchType) {
        var results = $(".otherSearchResults").length;
        try {
            var searchTerm = $("#tosinput").val();
            s.eVar1 = searchTerm;
            s.prop3 = searchTerm;
            // if there are search results fire event1
            if (results > 0) {
                s.prop4 = results;
                doOmnitureEvent("event1");
            }
                // if there are 0 search results fire event2
            else {
                s.prop4 = 'zero';
                doOmnitureEvent("event2");
            }
            //console.log("SearchType: " + SearchType + ", setNumber: " + setNumber + ", results: " + results + ", searchTerm: " + searchTerm);
        } catch (e) {
            console.log(e.message);
            console.log(e.name);
        }
    }

                }

            else {

                    tosinput();

            }
        }
        return true;
    });
    function hideKeyboard(element) {
        //console.log("hideKey2");
        element.attr('readonly', 'readonly'); // Force keyboard to hide on input field.
        element.attr('disabled', 'true'); // Force keyboard to hide on textarea field.
        setTimeout(function () {
            element.blur();  //actually close the keyboard
            // Remove readonly attribute after keyboard is hidden.
            element.removeAttr('readonly');
            element.removeAttr('disabled');
        }, 100);
    }

    var searchScrollY = 0;
    function searchScrollLoader() {
        //console.log("SRscrollTop: " + $("#tosearch").scrollTop() + " Results Height: " + $(".searchResults").height() + " searchScrollY: " + searchScrollY);
        if ($("#tosearch").scrollTop() >= searchScrollY + 100) {
            if (($("#tosearch").scrollTop() + 800) > $(".tosResultsBox").height()) {
                loadMoreResults();
            }
            searchScrollY = $("#tosearch").scrollTop();
        }
        SearchAndBooksItemViewable();
    }
    var SABIV_fired = false;
    function SearchAndBooksItemViewable() {
        if (SABIV_fired == false) {
            //console.log("SearchAndBooksItemViewable");
            SABIV_fired = true;
            var docViewTop = $(window).scrollTop();
            var docViewBottom = docViewTop + $(window).height();
            $(".TGN_RectBR_s5image").each(function (i, el) {
                var el = $(el);
                var elemTop = el.offset().top;
                var elemBottom = elemTop + 20;//el.height();
                if ((elemBottom <= docViewBottom) && (elemTop >= docViewTop)) {
                    el.css("background-image", "url('" + el.attr("data-url") + "')");
                }
            });
            setTimeout(function () {
                ResetSearchAndBooksItemViewable();
            }, 100);
        }
    }
    function ResetSearchAndBooksItemViewable() {
        SABIV_fired = false;
        TGNSearchLoadVisibleThumbs();
    }
    function loadMoreResults() {
        //console.log("From loadMore");
        var searchBox = $("#tosinput");
        searchTerm = searchBox.val();
        if (searchTerm !== "" && searchTerm !== null && searchTerm !== $('#tosinput').attr('placeholder')) {
            setNumber++;
            GetSearchResultArticleSet(validYearsString, setNumber, searchTerm, sortByType, sortByVideo);
            searchTermWas = searchTerm;
        } else {
            setNumber++;
            getSetBRArticles(validYearsString, setNumber, sortByVideo);
        }
    }

    function sortAsVideos(sortType) {
        //console.log("SAV: " + sortType);
        sortByVideo = sortType;
        curSortType = sortType;
        if (sortType == "all") {
            $(".SEARCHcolHead_Posts").css("border-bottom", "6px solid #3379be");
            $(".SEARCHcolHead_Videos").css("border-bottom", "6px solid #000");
        } else {
            $(".SEARCHcolHead_Videos").css("border-bottom", "6px solid #3379be");
            $(".SEARCHcolHead_Posts").css("border-bottom", "6px solid #000");
        }
        searchTermWas = "hcumgnihton";
        setNumber = 0;
    }

    <div id="AuthenticationHolder_FAQ_FAQcontent"><h1>Q. How do I create a Gates Notes account?</h1>
<h2>A. There are three ways you can create a Gates Notes account:</h2>

<ul><li><b>Sign up with Facebook.</b> We’ll never post to your Facebook account without your permission.</li>

<li><b>Sign up with Twitter.</b> We’ll never post to your Twitter account without your permission.</li>

<li><b>Sign up with your email.</b> Enter your email address during sign up. We’ll email you a link for verification.</li></ul>

<h1>Q. Will you ever post to my Facebook or Twitter accounts without my permission?</h1>
<h2>A. No, never.</h2>

<h1>Q. How do I sign up to receive email communications from my Gates Notes account?</h1>
<h2>A. In Account Settings, click the toggle switch next to “Send me updates from Bill Gates.”</h2>

<h1>Q. How will you use the Interests I select in Account Settings?</h1>
<h2>A. We will use them to choose the Suggested Reads that appear on your profile page.</h2></div>

           <div class='Awards_RazorRender_Holder' style='display:none;'><div class='Auth_SuggestedReads'>Awards</div><div class='Auth_SR_Holder' id='Auth_A_HolderR1'>

<script type="text/javascript">
    var TGNARR_currentUserActive = "false";
    var TGNARR_checkStatus = "false";
    var currentUserAwardsData = "";
    var TGNARR_CampaignUserPrizeData = [];
    var TGNARR_PrizelookInProgress = "false";

    $(document).ready(function () {
        setInterval(TGNARRInterval, 500);
    });
    function TGNARRInterval() {
        // check to see when user logs in
        if (TGNARR_currentUserActive != currentUserActive) {
            // change in user status detected
            TGNARR_currentUserActive = currentUserActive;
            if (currentUserActive == "true") {
                // user just logged IN
                // ajax call to see if this user has this award
                if (TGNARR_checkStatus == "false") {
                    // loop through prizes in TGNARR_CampaignUserPrizes
                    for (var i = 0, len = TGNARR_CampaignUserPrizes.length; i < len; i++) {
                        TGNARR_CampaignUserPrizeData = ItemStoreLookDataPrize = [];
                        lookGI(TGNARR_CampaignUserPrizes[i], "", "Prize", currentUserUserName);
                        TGNARR_PrizelookInProgress = "true";
                    }
                    //console.log("TURN END-POINT CALL ON IN Awards_RazorRender.cshtml");
                }
            } else {
                // user just logged OUT
                TGNARR_checkStatus = "false";
            }
        }
        if (ItemStoreLookDataPrize != TGNARR_CampaignUserPrizeData && TGNARR_PrizelookInProgress == "true") {
            TGNARR_CampaignUserPrizeData = ItemStoreLookDataPrize;
            if (currentUserActive == "true") {
                // we just got users Prize data
                TGNARR_PrizelookInProgress = "false";
                processUserPrizeDataARR();
            }
        }
    }

    function processUserPrizeDataARR() {
        for (var i = 0, len = TGNARR_CampaignUserPrizesEarned.length; i < len; i++) {
            TGNARR_ShowAwards(TGNARR_CampaignUserPrizesEarned[i]);
        }
    }

    function TGNARR_ShowAwards(Award) {
        // change to find based on items in TGNARR_CampaignUserPrizes

        $("#"+Award).css("display", "inline-block");
        $(".Awards_RazorRender_Holder").css("display", "block");
    }
</script>

<script type="text/javascript">

    $(document).ready(function () {
        console.log("Awards_RazorRender");
        // add to Prize list
        if ($.inArray("15db7e5c-b0c5-4167-b702-b248d4989ea0", TGNARR_CampaignUserPrizes) == -1) {
            TGNARR_CampaignUserPrizes.push("15db7e5c-b0c5-4167-b702-b248d4989ea0");
        }
        var TeaserString = $("#CoopDreams").find(".Auth_SR_Teaser").html();
        var decoded = $("<div/>").html(TeaserString).text();
        $("#CoopDreams").find(".Auth_SR_Teaser").html($.parseHTML(decoded));
        var datahtml = $("#CoopDreams").find(".Auth_SR_URL").text();
        var parsed = $('<div/>').append(datahtml);
        $("#CoopDreams").attr("href", parsed.find("a").attr("href"));
    });
</script></div></div>

<script type="text/javascript">
    var CampaignStartDate = Date.parse("8/13/2017 7:00:00 AM");
    var CampaignEndDate = Date.parse("10/15/2017 7:00:00 AM");
    var CampaignEnabled = $.parseJSON("True".toLowerCase());
    var TGNMag_currentUserActiveCTAs = "pending";
    var TGNMag_currentUserActiveCTAsCount = 0;
    $CTA_openHeight = 170;
    $(document).ready(function () {
        console.log("Magazine_SiteCTAsJS");
        if (CampaignStartDate > CampaignEndDate) {
            CampaignEnabled = false;
        }
        if (!CampaignEnabled) {
            //console.log("CampaignOver");
        } else {
            //console.log("----------------- CampaignOn -----------------");
        }
        // call to see if campaign is active
        if (CampaignEnabled && $(".ALS_Holder").length) {
            // if active show campaign CTA
            $(".ALS_Holder").append($("#TGNMag_CTAs_TopBannerParticipationCTA"));
            $(".ALS_Holder").append($("#TGNMag_CTAs_TopBannerSignUpCTA"));
        }
        function decodeHtml(html) {
            var txt = document.createElement("textarea");
            txt.innerHTML = html;
            return txt.value;
        }
        function TGNMag_gotoArticle(qs) {
            var tempDiv = document.createElement('div');
            tempDiv.innerHTML = decodeHtml("&lt;a href=&#39;/Health/Mosquito-Wars&#39; title=&#39;Coop Dreams Article&#39; &gt;Malaria Wars Article&lt;/a&gt;");
            tempDiv.setAttribute('style', 'display: none;');
            tempDiv.setAttribute('id', 'TGNMag_TempDiv');
            document.body.appendChild(tempDiv);
            if ($("#TGNMag_TempDiv").find("a").attr("href") != "" && $("#TGNMag_TempDiv").find("a").attr("href") != undefined) {
                if (qs == "") {
                    window.location.href = $("#TGNMag_TempDiv").find("a").attr("href");
                } else {
                    window.location.href = $("#TGNMag_TempDiv").find("a").attr("href") + "?showitem=" + qs;
                }
            }
        }
        $("#TGNMag_CTAs_LinkStyle_SU").click(function (e) {
            //window.location.href = "/signup";
            TGNMag_gotoArticle("signup");
        });
        $("#TGNMag_CTAs_LinkStyle_SI").click(function (e) {
            //window.location.href = "/signin";
            TGNMag_gotoArticle("signin");
        });
        $("#TGNMag_CTAs_LinkStyle_LM").click(function (e) {
            TGNMag_gotoArticle("learnmore");
        });
        $("#TGNMag_CTAs_LinkStyle_LM2").click(function (e) {
            TGNMag_gotoArticle("learnmore");
        });
        $("#TGNMag_CTAs_LinkStyle_ART").click(function (e) {
            TGNMag_gotoArticle("");
        });
    });
    $(window).resize(function () {
        updateMSCTAsWidth();
    });
    $('#tgnbody').scroll(function () {
        updateMSCTAsWidth();
    });
    function updateMSCTAsWidth() {
        var ww = $(window).width();
        var wh = $(window).height();
        var bh = 60;
        var scrollTopVal = $("#tgnbody").scrollTop();
    }
    setInterval(TGNMagIntervalCTAs, 500);
    function TGNMagIntervalCTAs() {
        if ($("#TGNMag_CTAs_TopBannerParticipationCTA").length || $("#TGNMag_CTAs_TopBannerSignUpCTA").length) {
            //$(".CTA_TDD_Holder").css("display", "none");
        }
        if (TGNMag_currentUserActiveCTAs != currentUserActive && CampaignEnabled) {
            // if user hasn't closed campaign CTA
            if (readALSCookie("MagCTA4") != "Closed" && readALSCookie("MagCTA5") != "Closed") {
                createALSCookie("ALSU", "ALS_override", 20 * 365);
            }
            $(".ALS_CloseX").css("color", "black");
            // change in user status detected
            //console.log("currentUserActiveMagCTAs: " + currentUserActive);
            //console.log("$('.ALS_Holder').height(): " + $(".ALS_Holder").height());
            TGNMag_currentUserActiveCTAsCount++;
            if (TGNMag_currentUserActiveCTAsCount > 6) {
                TGNMag_currentUserActiveCTAs = currentUserActive;
                TGNMag_currentUserActiveCTAsCount = 0;
            }
            if ($(".ALS_Holder").height() > 5) {
                TGNMag_currentUserActiveCTAs = currentUserActive;
                if (TGNMag_currentUserActiveCTAs == "true") {// && TGNMag_userEducated != "true"
                    // user just logged in
                    omnihelpers.setInsiderStatus(true);
                    // if logged in show TGNMag_CTAs_TopBannerParticipationCTA
                    $("#TGNMag_CTAs_TopBannerParticipationCTA").css("display", "block");
                    $("#TGNMag_CTAs_TopBannerSignUpCTA").css("display", "none");
                    $("#TGN_SU").css("opacity", "0");
                    $("#TGN_SU").css("height", "0");
                    $("#TGN_SU").css("pointer-events", "none");
                } else {
                    // user just logged out
                    omnihelpers.setInsiderStatus(false);
                    // if NOT logged in show TGNMag_CTAs_TopBannerSignUpCTA
                    $("#TGNMag_CTAs_TopBannerParticipationCTA").css("display", "none");
                    $("#TGNMag_CTAs_TopBannerSignUpCTA").css("display", "block");
                    $("#TGN_SU").css("opacity", "0");
                    $("#TGN_SU").css("height", "0");
                    $("#TGN_SU").css("pointer-events", "none");
                }
            } else {
                $("#TGNMag_CTAs_TopBannerParticipationCTA").css("display", "none");
                $("#TGNMag_CTAs_TopBannerSignUpCTA").css("display", "none");
            }
        }
    }
</script>

                //}
            }
            if (myPageName == "/books" && $(this).text().toLowerCase() == "books") {
                //$(this).css("font-family", "'HelveticaNeueW01-65Medi','Helvetica LT Std Light','Helvetica Neue LT Std',Helvetica");
                $(this).css("border-bottom", "4px solid rgb(166, 220, 243)");

                //if ($(this).parent().parent().parent().attr("id") == "TGN_BottomMenuS45_WordLinks") {
                //    //$(this).css("line-height", "41px");
                //}
            }
        });

        $(".TGN_BottomMenuS45FollowExpand_FBa").attr("href", $(".HeaderSiteShareFBa").attr('href'));

        // fix for IOS Touch items
        //$('a').on('click touchend', function (e) {

    function setBooksMobileNav(BPF_Set) {
        console.log("setBooksMobileNav: " + BPF_Set);
        BPF_Current = BPF_Set;
        if (BPF_Current != BPF_Prev) {
            $(".TGNBooksPageMobileTabletFC").each(function (i, obj) {
                if (i == BPF_Current) {
                    $(this).css("background-color", "#000000");
                    $(this).css("color", "#f3f3f3");
                    $(this).css("cursor", "auto");
                    $(this).css("pointer-events", "none");
                } else {
                    $(this).css("background-color", "#f3f3f3");
                    $(this).css("color", "#000000");
                    $(this).css("cursor", "pointer");
                    $(this).css("pointer-events", "all");
                }
                BPF_Prev = BPF_Current;
            });
        }
    }

    function TGN_MenuS45_ResetAnimProg() {
        TGN_MenuS45_AnimationInProgress = "false";
        setTimeout(function () {
            TGN_MenuS45_SizeScroll();
        }, 150);
    }
    function TGN_MenuS45_SizeScroll() {
        var TGN_MenuS45_NewMenuSize = false;
        $(".MenuS45_USERpop").css("display", "none");
        var wh = $(window).height();
        var ww = $(window).width();
        var scrollThreshold = 50;
        var scrollTopValH = $("#tgnbody").scrollTop();
        //console.log("scrollTopValH" + scrollTopValH);
        var scrollTopValPTH = 0;
        if ($(".promotitle").length) {
            var scrollTopValPTH = $(".promotitle").offset().top;
        }
        if ($(".artGalleryNBack").length) {
            var scrollTopValPTH = $(".artGalleryNBack").offset().top;
        }

        var mainSection = $("#mainSection");
        //we are in last section of article
        //console.log(scrollTopValPTH);
        if (scrollTopValPTH < wh) {
            $("#TGN_BottomMenuS45SharingCircleFb").css("background-image", "url('/TGN/img/TGN_badge_TransOutlines_C_Fb.svg')");
            $("#TGN_BottomMenuS45SharingCircleTw").css("background-image", "url('/TGN/img/TGN_badge_TransOutlines_C_Tw.svg')");
            $("#TGN_BottomMenuS45SharingCircleEm").css("background-image", "url('/TGN/img/TGN_badge_TransOutlines_C2_Em.svg')");
        } else {
            $("#TGN_BottomMenuS45SharingCircleFb").css("background-image", "url('/TGN/img/TGN_badge_TransOutlines_G_Fb.svg')");
            $("#TGN_BottomMenuS45SharingCircleTw").css("background-image", "url('/TGN/img/TGN_badge_TransOutlines_G_Tw.svg')");
            $("#TGN_BottomMenuS45SharingCircleEm").css("background-image", "url('/TGN/img/TGN_badge_TransOutlines_G_Em.svg')");
        }


        //TGN_TopMenuS45_SPHO = $("#socbannerProfileHeader_Holder").offset().top;
        $("#TGN_TopMenuS45_Left").css("width", ww+"px");
        if ($(".articleNext").is(':visible') || $("#NextArticle").length) {
        } else {
            $("#TGN_BottomMenuS45_Next").css("opacity", "0");
            $("#TGN_BottomMenuS45_Next").css("pointer-events", "none");
        }
        if (!$("#TGNLandingPageHolder").length || ww <= 980) {
            $(".headerDL").css("color", "#333");//767676
        }
        //$(".headerDL").css("margin-top", "0px");
        if (ww > 980) {
            $(".mobtonright").css("margin-top", "0px");
            //TGN_TopMenuS45_H = $("#socbanner").height();
            //TGN_TopMenuS45_H = 0;
            if (!$("#TGNLandingPageHolder").length) {
                $(".headerDL").css("color", "#fff");
            }
            if (scrollTopValH <= scrollThreshold) {
                TGN_TopMenuS45_H = 60;//60;//0 for overlap of header
                //$(".headerDL").css("text-transform", "capitalize");
                $("#LandingPage_Title").css("display", "block");
            } else {
                TGN_TopMenuS45_H = 40;//40;//0 for overlap of header
                //$(".headerDL").css("text-transform", "capitalize");
                //$(".headerDL").css("margin-top", "1px");
                $("#LandingPage_Title").css("display", "none");
            }
            TGN_MenuS45_State = "Desktop" + TGN_TopMenuS45_H;
        } else if (ww > 680) {
            if (scrollTopValH <= scrollThreshold && TGN_HeaderStyle == "NotAnArticle") {
                TGN_TopMenuS45_H = 100;
            } else {
                TGN_TopMenuS45_H = 60;
            }
            TGN_MenuS45_State = "Tablet" + TGN_TopMenuS45_H;
            $("#LandingPage_Title").css("display", "none");
        } else {
            if (scrollTopValH <= scrollThreshold && TGN_HeaderStyle == "NotAnArticle") {
                TGN_TopMenuS45_H = 68;
            } else {
                TGN_TopMenuS45_H = 40;
            }
            TGN_MenuS45_State = "Mobile" + TGN_TopMenuS45_H;
            $("#LandingPage_Title").css("display", "none");
            //$(".headerDL").css("margin-top", "2px");
        }
        $(".mobtonright").css("margin-top", TGN_TopMenuS45_H + "px");
        if (scrollTopValH <= scrollThreshold && (TGN_HeaderStyle == "NotAnArticle" || ww > 980)) {
            if (TGN_MenuS45_State != TGN_MenuS45_StateStored && TGN_MenuS45_AnimationInProgress == "false") {
                TGN_BottomMenuS45_hide();
                TGN_TopMenuS45_expand();
                TGN_MenuS45_StateStored = TGN_MenuS45_State;
                TGN_MenuS45_NewMenuSize = true;
            }
        } else {
            if (scrollTopValH <= scrollThreshold) {
                $("#TGN_TopMenuS45_Left_TBOBG").css("display", "inline-block");
                $("#TGN_TopMenuS45_Left_ArticleName").css("display", "none");
            } else {
                if (TGN_HeaderStyle != "NotAnArticle") {
                    $("#TGN_TopMenuS45_Left_TBOBG").css("display", "none");
                    $("#TGN_TopMenuS45_Left_ArticleName").css("display", "inline-block");
                }
            }
            if (TGN_MenuS45_State != TGN_MenuS45_StateStored && TGN_MenuS45_AnimationInProgress == "false") {
                if (ww > 980) {
                    TGN_BottomMenuS45_hide();
                } else {
                    TGN_BottomMenuS45_show();
                }
                TGN_BottomMenuS45_setLeft("close");
                TGN_BottomMenuS45_setRight("close");
                TGN_TopMenuS45_reduce();
                TGN_MenuS45_StateStored = TGN_MenuS45_State;
                TGN_MenuS45_NewMenuSize = true;
            }
        }
        // pos article name //17 31 45
        $("#TGN_TopMenuS45_Left_ArticleName").find("span").css('height', '');
        $("#TGN_TopMenuS45_Left_ArticleName").find("span").css('height', null);
        var myAN_H = $("#TGN_TopMenuS45_Left_ArticleName").find("span").height();
        //console.log("myAN_H: " + myAN_H);
        if (myAN_H > 40) {
            // 3 lines
            if (ww > 680) {
                $("#TGN_TopMenuS45_Left_ArticleName").css("top", "11px");
            } else {
                $("#TGN_TopMenuS45_Left_ArticleName").css("top", "6px");
            }
            $("#TGN_TopMenuS45_Left_ArticleName").find("span").css("height", "32px");
            $("#TGN_TopMenuS45_Left_ArticleName").find("span").css("line-height", "16px");
            $("#TGN_TopMenuS45_Left_ArticleName").find("span").css("overflow", "hidden");
            $("#TGN_TopMenuS45_Left_ArticleName").find("span").css("display", "inline-block");
        } else if (myAN_H > 28) {
            // 2 lines
            if (ww > 680) {
                $("#TGN_TopMenuS45_Left_ArticleName").css("top", "11px");
            } else {
                $("#TGN_TopMenuS45_Left_ArticleName").css("top", "6px");
            }
            $("#TGN_TopMenuS45_Left_ArticleName").find("span").css("height", "32px");
            $("#TGN_TopMenuS45_Left_ArticleName").find("span").css("line-height", "16px");
            $("#TGN_TopMenuS45_Left_ArticleName").find("span").css("overflow", "inline-block");
        } else if (myAN_H > 1) {
            // 1 line
            if (ww > 680) {
                $("#TGN_TopMenuS45_Left_ArticleName").css("top", "12px");
            } else {
                $("#TGN_TopMenuS45_Left_ArticleName").css("top", "5px");
            }
            $("#TGN_TopMenuS45_Left_ArticleName").find("span").css("height", "22px");
            $("#TGN_TopMenuS45_Left_ArticleName").find("span").css("line-height", "24px");
            $("#TGN_TopMenuS45_Left_ArticleName").find("span").css("overflow", "hidden");
            $("#TGN_TopMenuS45_Left_ArticleName").find("span").css("display", "inline-block");
        }
        //
        if (TGN_MenuS45_NewMenuSize == true) {
            TGN_MenuS45_NewMenuSize = false;
        }
        if (ww > 620) {
            $(".ALS_Inner_Holder").css("top", -20 + ($CTA_openHeight - $(".ALS_Inner_Holder").height()) / 2);
            $(".ALS_IL_Inner_Holder").css("top", -15 + ($(".ALS_IL_Holder").height() - $(".ALS_IL_Inner_Holder").height()) / 2);
        } else {
            $(".ALS_Inner_Holder").css("top", -3 + ($CTA_openHeight - $(".ALS_Inner_Holder").height()) / 2);
            $(".ALS_IL_Inner_Holder").css("top", 2 + ($(".ALS_IL_Holder").height() - $(".ALS_IL_Inner_Holder").height()) / 2);
        }


        setTGNBodyHeightMenuS45();
    }
    function setTGNBodyHeightMenuS45() {
            var wh = $(window).height();
            var ww = $(window).width();
            //console.log("wh" + wh + "TGN_TopMenuS45_H" + TGN_TopMenuS45_H + "TGN_BottomMenuS45_H" + TGN_BottomMenuS45_H);
            $("#tgnbody").css("height", (wh - TGN_TopMenuS45_H - TGN_BottomMenuS45_H) + "px");
            $(".AH_Holder").css("top", (TGN_TopMenuS45_H) + "px");
            $(".AH_Holder").css("height", (wh - TGN_TopMenuS45_H - TGN_BottomMenuS45_H) + "px");
            $(".tosearch").css("top", (TGN_TopMenuS45_H) + "px");
            $(".tosearch").css("height", (wh - TGN_TopMenuS45_H - TGN_BottomMenuS45_H) + "px");
            $(".TGN_TopMenuS45_Main_GNSimg").css("width", TGN_TopMenuS45_H + "px");
            $(".TGN_TopMenuS45_Main_GNSimg").css("height", TGN_TopMenuS45_H + "px");
            //$(".TGN_TopMenuS45_Main_GNSimg").css("top", $(".TGN_TopMenuS45_Left_GNSimg").offset().top + "px");
            $(".TGN_TopMenuS45_Main_GNSimg").css("left", $(".TGN_TopMenuS45_Left_GNSimg").offset().left + "px");
            $("#TGN_TopMenuS45_Main_Menu").css("width", $("#TGN_TopMenuS45_Right_Menu").width() + "px");
            $("#TGN_TopMenuS45_Main_Menu").css("height", $("#TGN_TopMenuS45_Right_Menu").height() + "px");
            $("#TGN_TopMenuS45_Main_Menu").css("top", $("#TGN_TopMenuS45_Right_Menu").offset().top + "px");
            $("#TGN_TopMenuS45_Main_Menu").css("left", $("#TGN_TopMenuS45_Right_Menu").offset().left + "px");
            if (TGN_TopMenuS45_H == 40) {
                $(".USERpop").css("top", (TGN_TopMenuS45_H + 10 + TGN_TopMenuS45_SPHO) + "px");
                $(".SIpop").css("top", (TGN_TopMenuS45_H + 10 + TGN_TopMenuS45_SPHO) + "px");
                if (ww <= 400) {
                    $("#TGN_TopMenuS45_Left").css("top", "-1px");
                } else {
                    $("#TGN_TopMenuS45_Left").css("top", "-2px");
                }
            } else {
                $(".USERpop").css("top", (TGN_TopMenuS45_H) + "px");
                $(".SIpop").css("top", (TGN_TopMenuS45_H) + "px");
                $("#TGN_TopMenuS45_Left").css("top", "0px");
            }
    }
    function TGN_BottomMenuS45_setLeft(mode) {
        //in out open
        switch (mode) {
            case "close":
                if (currentUserActive == "true") {
                    $("#TGN_BottomMenuS45_UserHeaderID").css("display", "block");
                    $("#TGN_BottomMenuS45_SignInHeaderID").css("display", "none");
                    $("#TGN_BottomMenuS45_SignIn_Close").css("display", "none");
                    $("#TGN_BottomMenuS45_SignIn").css("background-color", "#eee");
                    $("#TGN_TopMenuS45_LowerRight_UserHeaderID").css("display", "block");
                    $("#TGN_TopMenuS45_LowerRight_SignInHeaderID").css("display", "none");
                } else {
                    $("#TGN_BottomMenuS45_UserHeaderID").css("display", "none");
                    $("#TGN_BottomMenuS45_SignInHeaderID").css("display", "block");
                    $("#TGN_BottomMenuS45_SignIn_Close").css("display", "none");
                    $("#TGN_BottomMenuS45_SignIn").css("background-color", "#eee");
                    $("#TGN_TopMenuS45_LowerRight_UserHeaderID").css("display", "none");
                    $("#TGN_TopMenuS45_LowerRight_SignInHeaderID").css("display", "block");
                }
                break;
            case "open":
                $("#TGN_BottomMenuS45_UserHeaderID").css("display", "none");
                $("#TGN_BottomMenuS45_SignInHeaderID").css("display", "none");
                $("#TGN_BottomMenuS45_SignIn_Close").css("display", "block");
                $("#TGN_BottomMenuS45_SignIn").css("background-color", "#ccc");
                break;
        }
    }
    function TGN_BottomMenuS45_setRight(mode) {
        //follow next open
        switch (mode) {
            case "close":
                if (TGN_HeaderStyle == "NotAnArticle") {
                    //follow
                    $("#TGN_BottomMenuS45_Follow").css("display", "block");
                    $("#TGN_BottomMenuS45_Next").css("display", "none");
                    $("#TGN_BottomMenuS45_Right_Close").css("display", "none");
                    $("#TGN_BottomMenuS45_Right").css("background-color", "#eee");
                } else {
                    //next
                    $("#TGN_BottomMenuS45_Follow").css("display", "none");
                    $("#TGN_BottomMenuS45_Next").css("display", "block");
                    $("#TGN_BottomMenuS45_Right_Close").css("display", "none");
                    $("#TGN_BottomMenuS45_Right").css("background-color", "#eee");
                }
                break;
            case "open":
                $("#TGN_BottomMenuS45_Follow").css("display", "none");
                $("#TGN_BottomMenuS45_Next").css("display", "none");
                $("#TGN_BottomMenuS45_Right_Close").css("display", "block");
                $("#TGN_BottomMenuS45_Right").css("background-color", "#ccc");
                break;
        }
    }
    function TGN_BottomMenuS45_setCenter() {
        //console.log("TGN_HeaderStyle: "+TGN_HeaderStyle);
        if (TGN_HeaderStyle == "NotAnArticle") {
            //words
            $("#TGN_BottomMenuS45_WordLinks").css("display", "block");
            $("#TGN_BottomMenuS45_Sharing").css("display", "none");
        } else {
            //share
            $("#TGN_BottomMenuS45_Sharing").css("display", "block");
            $("#TGN_BottomMenuS45_WordLinks").css("display", "none");
        }
    }
    function TGN_BottomMenuS45_show() {
        AnimTGN_BottomMenuS45Holder(0);
        TGN_BottomMenuS45_H = 60;
    }
    function TGN_BottomMenuS45_hide() {
        AnimTGN_BottomMenuS45Holder(-60);
        TGN_BottomMenuS45_setLeft("close");
        TGN_BottomMenuS45_setRight("close");
        TGN_BottomMenuS45_H = 0;
    }
    $("#TGN_BottomMenuS45_UserHeaderID").click(function () {
        TGN_BottomMenuS45_openSI();
        TGN_BottomMenuS45_H = 150;
        setTGNBodyHeightMenuS45();
    });
    function MenuS45_OpenSignIn() {
        if ($(".Login_Holder").is(':visible')) {
            hideAuthHolders();
        } else {
            hideAuthHolders();
            $(".AH_Holder").css("display", "block");
            $(".Login_Holder").css("display", "block");
            omnihelpers.loginStart();
            $(".SIpop").css("display", "none");
            $("#AuthenticationHolder_Login_txtEmail").val('');
            $("#AuthenticationHolder_Login_chkPersist").val('');
            $("#AuthenticationHolder_Login_txtPassword").val('');
            $("#LI_Mob_All_Error").css("display", "none");
        }
    }
    $("#TGN_BottomMenuS45_SignInHeaderID").click(function () {
        MenuS45_OpenSignIn();
    });
    $("#TGN_BottomMenuS45_SignIn_Close").click(function () {
        TGN_BottomMenuS45_closeSI();
        TGN_BottomMenuS45_H = 60;
        setTGNBodyHeightMenuS45();
    });
    $("#TGN_BottomMenuS45_Follow").click(function () {
        TGN_BottomMenuS45_openFollow();
        TGN_BottomMenuS45_H = 120;
        setTGNBodyHeightMenuS45();
    });
    $("#TGN_BottomMenuS45_Right_Close").click(function () {
        TGN_BottomMenuS45_closeFollow();
        TGN_BottomMenuS45_H = 60;
        setTGNBodyHeightMenuS45();
    });
    $("#TGN_TopMenuS45_LowerRight_SignInHeaderID").click(function () {
        MenuS45_OpenSignIn();
    });
    $("#TGN_BottomMenuS45_Next").click(function () {
        if ($(".articleNext").is(':visible')) {
            location.href = $(".articleNext").attr('href');
        } else if ($("#NextArticle").is(':visible')) {
            location.href = $("#content_0_articleGallery_NextArticleLink").attr('href');
        }
    });
