    // open User expand
    function TGN_BottomMenuS45_openSI() {
        AnimTGN_BottomMenuS45Holder(90);
        $("#TGN_BottomMenuS45SignInExpand").css("display", "block");
        $("#TGN_BottomMenuS45FollowExpand").css("display", "none");
        TGN_BottomMenuS45_setLeft("open");
        TGN_BottomMenuS45_setRight("close");
        $(".USERpop").css("display", "none");
        $(".USERpop").css("opacity", "0");
        $(".USERpop").css("pointer-events", "none");
    }
    // close User expand
    function TGN_BottomMenuS45_closeSI() {
        AnimTGN_BottomMenuS45Holder(0);
        $("#TGN_BottomMenuS45SignInExpand").delay(0).css("display", "none");
        $("#TGN_BottomMenuS45FollowExpand").delay(0).css("display", "none");
        TGN_BottomMenuS45_setLeft("close");
        $(".USERpop").css("display", "none");
        $(".USERpop").css("opacity", "1");
        $(".USERpop").css("pointer-events", "all");
    }
    // open follow expand //60px
    function TGN_BottomMenuS45_openFollow() {
        AnimTGN_BottomMenuS45Holder(60);
        $("#TGN_BottomMenuS45SignInExpand").css("display", "none");
        $("#TGN_BottomMenuS45FollowExpand").css("display", "block");
        TGN_BottomMenuS45_setRight("open");
        TGN_BottomMenuS45_setLeft("close");
    }
    // close follow expand
    function TGN_BottomMenuS45_closeFollow() {
        AnimTGN_BottomMenuS45Holder(0);
        $("#TGN_BottomMenuS45SignInExpand").delay(0).css("display", "none");
        $("#TGN_BottomMenuS45FollowExpand").delay(0).css("display", "none");
        TGN_BottomMenuS45_setRight("close");
    }
    // user signed in
    function TGN_BottomMenuS45_SI() {
        TGN_BottomMenuS45_setLeft("close");
        $("#TGN_TopMenuS45_Main_Menu_MyProfile").css("display", "block");
        $("#TGN_TopMenuS45_Main_Menu_Logout").css("display", "block");
    }
    // user signed out
    function TGN_BottomMenuS45_SO() {
        TGN_BottomMenuS45_setLeft("close");
        $("#TGN_TopMenuS45_Main_Menu_MyProfile").css("display", "none");
        $("#TGN_TopMenuS45_Main_Menu_Logout").css("display", "none");
    }
    function AnimTGN_BottomMenuS45Holder(bottom) {
        $("#TGN_BottomMenuS45Holder").stop();
        $("#TGN_BottomMenuS45Holder").clearQueue();
        $("#TGN_BottomMenuS45Holder").delay(0).animate({ 'bottom': bottom + 'px' }, TGN_AnimationTime);
    }
    function TGN_BottomMenuS45scrollToComments() {
        var scrollTopValH = $("#tgnbody").scrollTop();
        var scrollTopComVal = $(".newComments").offset().top;
        $("#tgnbody").delay(0).animate({ scrollTop: scrollTopValH + scrollTopComVal - 120 }, TGN_AnimationTime);
    }
</script>

       function scrollVidWidget() {
           var see = $("#tgnbody").scrollTop();
           var t = parseInt($(".socbanner").css("height"), 10);
           if ((t + see + vidHeight) < 564) {
               $(".heroOverlay").css("position", "fixed");
               $(".heroOverlay").css("top", t + "px");
           }
           else {
               $(".heroOverlay").css("position", "inherit");//absolute
               $(".heroOverlay").css("top", (564-vidHeight) + "px");
           }
       }

<script type="text/javascript">
    var showshares = true;
    var commentTry = 0;

    var swfbshares = 0;
    var swtwshares = 0;
    var swlishares = 0;
    var swfbshares2 = 0;
    var swtwshares2 = 0;
    var swlishares2 = 0;
    var swcomments = 0;

    function addshare(d, d2, alt) {
        if (d == null || d == undefined || d == 0)
            d = 0;
        if (d2 == null || d2 == undefined || d2 == 0)
            d2 = 0;
        d = d + d2;
        if (d == 0)
            return alt;
        var back = d + " SHARE";
        if (d != 1)
            back += "S";
        return back;
    }
    function addcomment(d) {
        if (d == 0)
            return;
        var back = d + " COMMENT";
        if (d != 1)
            back += "S";
        return back;
    }
    function populateWidget() {
        if (showshares) {
            $(".scoshare").html(addcomment(swcomments));
            $(".stwshare").html(addshare(swtwshares, swtwshares2, "TWEET"));
            $(".sfbshare").html(addshare(swfbshares, swfbshares2, "SHARE"));
            $(".slishare").html(addshare(swlishares, swlishares2, "SHARE"));
            
        }
    }

        });
        $(".emShare").click(function () {
            s.eVar9 = "email";
            s.eVar14 = document.title;
            doOmnitureEvent("event11");
        });
        function doOmnitureEvent(event) {
            try {
                s.linkTrackVars = "events,eVar9,eVar14";
                s.linkTrackEvents = "event11";
                s.events = event;
                s.tl(true, 'o', 'article');
            } catch (e) {
                console.log(e.message);
                console.log(e.name);
            }
        }
    });
</script>

<script type="text/javascript">
    //
    //// Homepage animations
    //
    var curAnim = null;
    var curThumb = null;
    var thumbList = [];
    // test for visible thumbnails
    function findAvailThumb() {
        var ww = $(window).width();
        if (ww > 980) {
            //console.log("FAT");
            thumbList = [];
            $(".hpimgrel").each(function (index) {
                var offsetA = $(this).offset();
                //console.log("ww:" + $(window).width() + " wh:" + $(window).height() + " thisOff:" + offsetA.top + " i:" + index + " scrollTop:" + $("#tgnbody").scrollTop());
                if (offsetA.top > -70 && offsetA.top < $(window).height() - 210) {

                    // find available thumbnails
                    if ($(this).find(".thumbVideoHolder").length) {
                        thumbList.push($(this));
                        //console.log("found");
                        //// hide jpg thumb
                        //$(this).find(".searchthumb").css("display", "none");
                        //curThumb = $(this).find(".searchthumb");
                        //// show video thumb
                        //$(this).find(".thumbVideoHolder").css("display", "block");
                        //curAnim = $(this).find(".thumbVideoHolder");
                        // play video
                        //$(this).find(".thumbVideo").get(0).play();
                    }
                    //console.log("visible:" + Math.floor(index + 1));
                }
                //oy > -140 and oy < wh-140

            });
            //console.log("pool: " + thumbList.length);
            if (thumbList.length > 0) {
                var item = thumbList[Math.floor(Math.random() * thumbList.length)];
                // hide jpg thumb
                item.find(".searchthumb").css("display", "none");
                curThumb = item.find(".searchthumb");
                // show video thumb
                item.find(".thumbVideoHolder").css("display", "block");
                curAnim = item.find(".thumbVideoHolder");
                item.find(".thumbVideo").get(0).play();
            } else {
                setTimeout(function () {
                    findAvailThumb();
                }, 4000);
            }
        }
        
    }
    // run 1 random animation from pool
    // listen for end of animation OR set amount of time for looping
    function videoEnded() {
        //console.log("video end");
        curThumb.css("display", "block");
        curAnim.css("display", "none");
    // pause for time between animations
        setTimeout(function () {
            findAvailThumb();
        }, 4000);
        //findAvailThumb();
    }
    $(document).ready(function () {
        setTimeout(function () {
            findAvailThumb();
        }, 4000);

        $("#tgnbody").scroll(function () {
            var animscrollTopVal = $("#tgnbody").scrollTop();
            //console.log(animscrollTopVal)
            // test on scroll if active item is still visible
            if (animscrollTopVal === 0) {
            } else {
            }
        });
    });
    //
    //// End Homepage animations
    //
</script>

<script type="text/javascript">
    TGN_Page_Style = "home";
    var BR_ImageRatio = 800 / 493;
    var LPV_Prev = 9;
    var LPV_Current = 0;
    var PopularLoaded = false;
    var VideosLoaded = false;
    $(document).ready(function () {
        console.log("TGNHomePage_JS");
        GetHomePageVideosArticleSet("2020,2019,2018,2017,2016,2015,2014,2013,2012,2011,2010,2009", 0, "", "date", "video");
        //$(".herohero").css("background-image", "url(\"" + $("#TGN_RectBR_s1imageHero").css("background-image") + "\")");
        $(".herohero").css("background-image", "" + $("#TGN_RectBR_s1imageHero").css("background-image") + "");
        // add Hero image to area where it can go full width
        var a = document.createElement('a');
        $(a).attr('href', $("#TGNHomePageMobileTabletHero1").find("a").attr("href")).attr('id', 'TGN_RectBR_s1imageHeroMobLink');
        var b = $("#TGN_RectBR_s1imageHero").clone().attr("id", "TGN_RectBR_s1imageHeroMob");
        $(a).append(b);
        $(a).insertAfter(".heroHolder");
        //$("#TGNHomePageMobileTabletPopular").prepend($("#TopStories_TopStoriesHolder"));
        loadHomePageRecentArticleList();
        IS_IPAD = navigator.userAgent.match(/iPad/i) != null;
        IS_IPHONE = (navigator.userAgent.match(/iPhone/i) != null) || (navigator.userAgent.match(/iPod/i) != null);
        if (IS_IPAD) {
            IS_IPHONE = false;
        }
        //var tap = ("ontouchstart" in document.documentElement);
        if(!IS_IPAD && !IS_IPHONE){
            $(".hpunit").mouseenter(function () {
                $(this).find(".hpheadline").css("text-decoration","underline");
                if ($(this).find(".searchthumb").length) {
                    $(this).find(".TGN_searchthumbimageDATE").css("display","block");
                    $(this).find(".TGN_searchthumbimageCTA").css("display","block");
                    var ww = $(window).width();
                    if (ww > 680) {
                        TGN_s47_Black_RollOver($(this).find(".searchthumb"));
                    }
                }
            });
            $(".hpunit").mouseleave(function () {
                $(this).find(".hpheadline").css("text-decoration","none");
                if ($(this).find(".searchthumb").length) {
                    $(this).find(".TGN_searchthumbimageDATE").css("display","none");
                    $(this).find(".TGN_searchthumbimageCTA").css("display","none");
                    TGN_DarkVignetteRollOut($(this).find(".searchthumb"));
                }
            });
        }
        // image rollovers
        function TGN_s47_Black_RollOver(canvas) {
            var ctx = canvas.get(0).getContext("2d");
            var width = ctx.canvas.width;
            var height = ctx.canvas.height;
            var width2 = canvas.width();
            var height2 = canvas.height();
            var pixels = ctx.getImageData(0, 0, width, height);
            ctx.putImageData(pixels, 0, 0);
            outerRadius = Math.sqrt(Math.pow(width / 2, 2) + Math.pow(height / 2, 2));
            ctx.globalCompositeOperation = 'source-over';
            gradient = ctx.createRadialGradient(width / 2, height / 2, 0, width / 2, height / 2, outerRadius);
            gradient.addColorStop(0, 'rgba(0,0,0,.65)');
            gradient.addColorStop(1, 'rgba(0,0,0,.65)');
            ctx.fillStyle = gradient;
            ctx.fillRect(0, 0, width, height);
            //
            //canvas.parent().find(".TGN_RectBR_s4imageDATEtext").html(canvas.attr("data-dateattr"));
            canvas.parent().find(".TGN_RectBR_s4imageDATEtext").attr("data-dateval",canvas.attr("data-dateval"));
            canvas.parent().find(".TGN_RectBR_s4imageDATE").css("display","block");
            canvas.parent().find(".TGN_RectBR_s4imageDATE").css("margin-top",-height2*0.92+"px");
            canvas.parent().find(".TGN_RectBR_s4imageDATE").css("margin-left",height2*0.1+"px");
            canvas.parent().find(".TGN_RectBR_s4imageDATE").css("font-size",height2*0.061+"px");
            canvas.parent().find(".TGN_RectBR_s4imageCTAtext").html(canvas.attr("data-ctaattr"));
            canvas.parent().find(".TGN_RectBR_s4imageCTA").css("display","block");
            canvas.parent().find(".TGN_RectBR_s4imageCTA").css("margin-top",-height2*0.24+"px");
            canvas.parent().find(".TGN_RectBR_s4imageCTA").css("margin-left",height2*0.1+"px");
            canvas.parent().find(".TGN_RectBR_s4imageCTA").css("font-size",height2*0.113043478+"px");
            canvas.parent().find(".TGN_RectBR_s4imageCTA").css("height",height2*0.15+"px");
        }
        function TGN_DarkVignetteRollOut(canvas) {
            //
            var ctx = canvas.get(0).getContext("2d");
            var width = ctx.canvas.width;
            var height = ctx.canvas.height;
            var img = new Image();
            img.src = "";
            ctx.save();
            ctx.setTransform(1, 0, 0, 1, 0, 0);
            ctx.clearRect(0, 0, width, height);
            ctx.restore();
            img.onload = function () {
                ctx.drawImage(img, 0, 0);
            };
            canvas.parent().find(".TGN_RectBR_s4imageDATE").css("display","none");
            canvas.parent().find(".TGN_RectBR_s4imageCTA").css("display","none");
        }
        //var tap = ("ontouchstart" in document.documentElement);
        if(!IS_IPAD && !IS_IPHONE){
            $(".TGN_RectBR_s4").mouseenter(function () {
                $(this).find(".TGN_RectBR_s4title").css("text-decoration","underline");
                var ww = $(window).width();
                if (ww > 680) {
                    TGN_s47_Black_RollOver($(this).find(".TGN_RectBR_s4image"));
                }
            });
            $(".TGN_RectBR_s4").mouseleave(function () {
                $(this).find(".TGN_RectBR_s4title").css("text-decoration","none");
                TGN_DarkVignetteRollOut($(this).find(".TGN_RectBR_s4image"));
            });
        }
    });
    $(window).resize(function () {
        updateTGNHomePage();
        TGNHomeLoadThumbnails();
    });
    $('#tgnbody').scroll(function () {
        //updateTGNHomePage();
        TGNHomeLoadThumbnails();
    });
    function TGNHomeLoadThumbnails() {
        $(".searchthumb").each(function (i, obj) {
            if ($(this).is(':visible') && TGNHomeisOnScreen($(this))) {
                if ($(this).attr("data-url") != "set") {
                    $(this).css("background-image", "url('"+$(this).attr("data-url")+"')");
                    $(this).parent().find(".thumbVideoSource").attr("src", $(this).parent().find(".thumbVideoSource").attr("data-url"));
                    $(this).parent().find(".thumbVideoSource").attr("data-url", "set");
                    var video = $(this).parent().find(".thumbVideo");
                    video.load();
                    $(this).attr("data-url", "set");
                }
            }
        });
        $(".TGN_RectBR_s4image").each(function (i, obj) {
            if ($(this).is(':visible') && TGNHomeisOnScreen($(this))) {
                if ($(this).attr("data-url") != "set") {
                    $(this).css("background-image", "url('"+$(this).attr("data-url")+"')");
                    $(this).attr("data-url", "set");
                }
            }
        });
        $(".hpimgrel").each(function (i, obj) {
            if ($(this).is(':visible') && TGNHomeisOnScreen($(this))) {
                if ($(this).attr("data-url") != "set") {
                    $("<img src='"+$(this).attr("data-url")+"' class='hpSearchImageBook' alt='"+$(this).attr("data-alt")+"'>").insertBefore($(this).find(".gbox"));
                    $(this).attr("data-url", "set");
                }
            }
        });
    }
    function TGNHomeisOnScreen(element)
    {
        var curPos = element.offset();
        var curTop = curPos.top;
        var screenHeight = $(window).height();
        return (curTop > screenHeight) ? false : true;
    }
    function updateTGNHomePage() {
        var ww = $(window).width();
        var wh = $(window).height();
        var tallestTGN_RectBR_s4 = 0;
        if (ww > 980) {
            nohero = false;
            $(".heroHolder").css("margin-top", 0 + "px");
        } else {
            nohero = true;
            $(".heroHolder").css("margin-top", -$(".heroHolder").height() + "px");
        }
        $("#TGN_RectBR_s1imageHeroMob").css("width", (ww) + "px");
        $("#TGN_RectBR_s1imageHeroMob").css("height", ($("#TGN_RectBR_s1imageHeroMob").width() / BR_ImageRatio) + "px");
        $(".TGN_RectBR_s4").each(function (i, obj) {
            if (ww > 680) {


                var idstr = $(obj).attr("id");
                var index = idstr.charAt(idstr.length - 1);
                //use the index that is on the id and not rely on counts of objects on the page
                
                if (!isNaN(index)) {
                    i = index;
                }
                if (i % 2 === 0) {
                    
                    /* we are even */
                    $(this).css("float", "left");
                    $(this).css("margin-right", "10px");
                    $(this).css("clear", "both");
                }
                else {
                    /* we are odd */
                    $(this).css("float", "right");
                    $(this).css("margin-right", "0px");
                }
                $(this).css("width", +(ww - 70-9) / 2 + "px");
            } else {
                $(this).css("float", "none");
                $(this).css("margin-right", "0px");
                $(this).css("width", "100%");
            }
            tallestTGN_RectBR_s4 = Math.max(tallestTGN_RectBR_s4, $(this).height());
        });
        $(".TGN_RectBR_s4image").each(function (i, obj) {
            $(this).css("height", + ($(this).width()/BR_ImageRatio) + "px");
        });
        // Make Heights Uniform
        //$(".TGN_RectBR_s4").each(function (i, obj) {
        //    $(this).css("height", +(tallestTGN_RectBR_s4) + "px");
        //});
        $("#TGNHomePageMobileTabletCTA").css("width", ww+"px");
    }
    function setLPV(LPV_Set) {
        //console.log("setLPV:" + LPV_Set);
        LPV_Current = LPV_Set;
        if (LPV_Current != LPV_Prev) {
            $(".TGNHomePageMobileTabletAC").each(function (i, obj) {
                if (i == LPV_Current) {
                    $(this).css("background-color", "#000000");
                    $(this).css("color", "#f3f3f3");
                    $(this).css("cursor", "auto");
                    $(this).css("pointer-events", "none");
                } else {
                    $(this).css("background-color", "#f3f3f3");
                    $(this).css("color", "#000000");
                    $(this).css("cursor", "pointer");
                    $(this).css("pointer-events", "all");
                }
                LPV_Prev = LPV_Current;
            });
            switch (LPV_Set) {
                case 0:
                    $("#TGNHomePageMobileTabletLatest").css("display", "block");
                    $("#TGNHomePageMobileTabletPopular").css("display", "none");
                    $("#TGNHomePageMobileTabletVideos").css("display", "none");
                    break;
                case 1:
                    $("#TGNHomePageMobileTabletLatest").css("display", "none");
                    $("#TGNHomePageMobileTabletPopular").css("display", "block");
                    $("#TGNHomePageMobileTabletVideos").css("display", "none");
                    break;
                case 2:
                    $("#TGNHomePageMobileTabletLatest").css("display", "none");
                    $("#TGNHomePageMobileTabletPopular").css("display", "none");
                    $("#TGNHomePageMobileTabletVideos").css("display", "block");
                    break;
            }
            updateTGNHomePage();
            TGNHomeLoadThumbnails();
        }
    }
    $("#TGNHomePageMobileTabletACL").click(function () {
        setLPV(0);
    });
    $("#TGNHomePageMobileTabletACP").click(function () {
        setLPV(1);
    });
    $("#TGNHomePageMobileTabletACV").click(function () {
        setLPV(2);
    });
    // Get a particular set of articles from the blogroll within specified years - Matching a specified SEARCH TERM
    function GetHomePageVideosArticleSet() {
        $.ajax({
            url: "/tgnservices/BlogRollService.asmx/GetBlogRollArticleSet?validYearsString=2020,2019,2018,2017,2016,2015,2014,2013,2012,2011,2010,2009&setNumber=0&sortByVideo=video",
            dataType: "json",
            type: "GET",
            success: function (data) {
                for (var i = 0; i < data.ArticleList.length; i++) {
                    $("#TGNHomePageMobileTabletVideos").append("<div id='TGNHomePageMobileTabletVideos" + i + "' class='TGN_RectBR_s4'><a href='" + data.ArticleList[i].ArticleUrl + "'><canvas id='TGN_RectBR_s4imageV" + i + "' data-dateval='" + data.ArticleList[i].Date + "' data-url='" + data.ArticleList[i].ImageUrl + "' class='TGN_RectBR_s4image' style='position: relative; width: 100%; overflow-x: hidden; opacity: 1; background-image: url(&quot;&quot;); background-size: cover; background-position: 50% 50%; background-repeat: no-repeat;'></canvas><div class='TGN_RectBR_s4imageDATE'><span class='TGN_RectBR_s4imageDATEtext'>" + data.ArticleList[i].RollOverDate + "</span></div><div class='TGN_RectBR_s4imageCTA'><span class='TGN_RectBR_s4imageCTAtext'>" + data.ArticleList[i].BlogrollCTATag + "</span></div><div class='TGN_RectBR_s4title'>" + data.ArticleList[i].Headline + "</div><div class='TGN_RectBR_s4blurb'>" + data.ArticleList[i].SearchBlurb + "</div><div class='TGN_RectBR_s4date'>" + data.ArticleList[i].Date + "</div></a></div>");
                }
                //console.log(data);
                IS_IPAD = navigator.userAgent.match(/iPad/i) != null;
                IS_IPHONE = (navigator.userAgent.match(/iPhone/i) != null) || (navigator.userAgent.match(/iPod/i) != null);
                if (IS_IPAD) {
                    IS_IPHONE = false;
                }
                //var tap = ("ontouchstart" in document.documentElement);
                if(!IS_IPAD && !IS_IPHONE){
                    $(".TGN_RectBR_s4").mouseenter(function () {
                        $(this).find(".TGN_RectBR_s4title").css("text-decoration","underline");
                        var ww = $(window).width();
                        if (ww > 680) {
                            TGN_s47_Black_RollOver($(this).find(".TGN_RectBR_s4image"));
                        }
                        //TGN_s47_Black_RollOver($(this).find(".TGN_RectBR_s4image"));
                    });
                    $(".TGN_RectBR_s4").mouseleave(function () {
                        $(this).find(".TGN_RectBR_s4title").css("text-decoration","none");
                        TGN_DarkVignetteRollOut($(this).find(".TGN_RectBR_s4image"));
                    });
                }
                function TGN_s47_Black_RollOver(canvas) {
                    var ctx = canvas.get(0).getContext("2d");
                    var width = ctx.canvas.width;
                    var height = ctx.canvas.height;
                    var width2 = canvas.width();
                    var height2 = canvas.height();
                    var pixels = ctx.getImageData(0, 0, width, height);
                    ctx.putImageData(pixels, 0, 0);
                    outerRadius = Math.sqrt(Math.pow(width / 2, 2) + Math.pow(height / 2, 2));
                    ctx.globalCompositeOperation = 'source-over';
                    gradient = ctx.createRadialGradient(width / 2, height / 2, 0, width / 2, height / 2, outerRadius);
                    gradient.addColorStop(0, 'rgba(0,0,0,.65)');
                    gradient.addColorStop(1, 'rgba(0,0,0,.65)');
                    ctx.fillStyle = gradient;
                    ctx.fillRect(0, 0, width, height);
                    //
                    //canvas.parent().find(".TGN_RectBR_s4imageDATEtext").html(canvas.attr("data-dateattr"));
                    canvas.parent().find(".TGN_RectBR_s4imageDATEtext").attr("data-dateval",canvas.attr("data-dateval"));
                    canvas.parent().find(".TGN_RectBR_s4imageDATE").css("display","block");
                    canvas.parent().find(".TGN_RectBR_s4imageDATE").css("margin-top",-height2*0.92+"px");
                    canvas.parent().find(".TGN_RectBR_s4imageDATE").css("margin-left",height2*0.1+"px");
                    canvas.parent().find(".TGN_RectBR_s4imageDATE").css("font-size",height2*0.061+"px");
                    canvas.parent().find(".TGN_RectBR_s4imageCTAtext").html(canvas.attr("data-ctaattr"));
                    canvas.parent().find(".TGN_RectBR_s4imageCTA").css("display","block");
                    canvas.parent().find(".TGN_RectBR_s4imageCTA").css("margin-top",-height2*0.24+"px");
                    canvas.parent().find(".TGN_RectBR_s4imageCTA").css("margin-left",height2*0.1+"px");
                    canvas.parent().find(".TGN_RectBR_s4imageCTA").css("font-size",height2*0.113043478+"px");
                    canvas.parent().find(".TGN_RectBR_s4imageCTA").css("height",height2*0.15+"px");
                }
                function TGN_DarkVignetteRollOut(canvas) {
                    //
                    var ctx = canvas.get(0).getContext("2d");
                    var width = ctx.canvas.width;
                    var height = ctx.canvas.height;
                    var img = new Image();
                    img.src = "";
                    ctx.save();
                    ctx.setTransform(1, 0, 0, 1, 0, 0);
                    ctx.clearRect(0, 0, width, height);
                    ctx.restore();
                    img.onload = function () {
                        ctx.drawImage(img, 0, 0);
                    };
                    canvas.parent().find(".TGN_RectBR_s4imageDATE").css("display","none");
                    canvas.parent().find(".TGN_RectBR_s4imageCTA").css("display","none");
                }
                VideosLoaded = true;
                if (VideosLoaded && PopularLoaded) {
                    setupThumbnailRollovers();
                }
                updateTGNHomePage();
            }
        });
    }

    function setupThumbnailRollovers() {
        $(".searchthumb").each(function (i, obj) {
            $(this).parent().find(".TGN_searchthumbimageDATEtext").html($(this).attr("data-dateattr"));
            $(this).parent().find(".TGN_searchthumbimageDATEtext").attr("data-dateval",$(this).attr("data-dateval"));
            $(this).parent().find(".TGN_searchthumbimageCTAtext").html($(this).attr("data-ctaattr"));
        });
        $(".TGN_RectBR_s4image").each(function (i, obj) {
            $(this).parent().find(".TGN_RectBR_s4imageDATEtext").html($(this).attr("data-dateattr"));
            $(this).parent().find(".TGN_RectBR_s4imageDATEtext").attr("data-dateval",$(this).attr("data-dateval"));
            $(this).parent().find(".TGN_RectBR_s4imageCTAtext").html($(this).attr("data-ctaattr"));
        });
        $(".TGN_RectBR_s4imageDATEtext").each(function (i, obj) {
            var d = $.datepicker.parseDate("MM dd, yy",  $(this).attr("data-dateval"));
            var Today = new Date();
            var dayCount = Calculatedays(d,Today);
            var RollOverDate = CalculateRollOverDate(dayCount);
            $(this).html(RollOverDate);
        });
        $(".TGN_searchthumbimageDATEtext").each(function (i, obj) {
            var RollOverDate = GetRolloverDate($(this).attr("data-dateval"));
            $(this).html(RollOverDate);
        });
    }
</script>

    var isHomePage = true ;
    var pageId = '{110D559F-DEA5-42EA-9C1C-8A5DF7E70EF9}';    
	var disqus_shortname = window.location.host === 'www.gatesnotes.com' ? 'thegatesnotes' : 'ppethegatesnotes';
    var articles;
    function bindOmnitureEvents(){
        $(".fbhover:not(.bound)").addClass("bound").click(fbEvent);
        $(".twhover:not(.bound)").addClass("bound").click(twEvent);
        $(".lihover:not(.bound)").addClass("bound").click(liEvent);
        $(".icon-mail_4:not(.bound)").addClass("bound").click(emEvent);
        function fbEvent(){
            var articleTitle = $(this).closest(".gosocov").attr("data-id");
            s.eVar14 = articleTitle;
            s.eVar9 = "facebook";
            doOmnitureEvent("event11");
        }
        function twEvent(){
            var articleTitle = $(this).closest(".gosocov").attr("data-id");
            s.eVar14 = articleTitle;
            s.eVar9 = "twitter";
            doOmnitureEvent("event11");
        }
        function liEvent(){
            var articleTitle = $(this).closest(".gosocov").attr("data-id");
            s.eVar14 = articleTitle;
            s.eVar9 = "linkedin";
            doOmnitureEvent("event11");
        }
        function emEvent(){
            var articleTitle = $(this).closest(".gosocov").attr("data-id");
            s.eVar14 = articleTitle;
            s.eVar9 = "email";
            doOmnitureEvent("event11");
        }
        function doOmnitureEvent(event) {
            try {
                s.linkTrackVars = "events,eVar9,eVar14";
                s.linkTrackEvents = "event11";
                s.events = event;
                s.tl(true, 'o', 'article');
            } catch (e) {
                console.log(e.message);
                console.log(e.name);
            }
        }
    }
    var lastwidth = 0;
    var $mobilehomepage = 620; //480;
    $(document).ready(function () {

        //getArticles();
        //watchScroll(); 
        lastwidth =  $(window).width();
        if (!isHomePage || (lastwidth < $mobilehomepage))
        {
            hidehomepage();
         }
        $(".loadMorePosts").click(function () {
            animloadmore();
        });

    });
    function hidehomepage () {
        $(".homepage").hide();
        $(".thePosts").show();
        if (firstload) {
            // don't do the load SES loadMorePosts();       
            DisqusCommentsCounter();
            /* // ses remove LMP 
            $(".loadMorePosts").click(function () {
                animloadmore();
            });
            */
        }
    };
    function showhomepage () {
        $(".homepage").show();
        $(".thePosts").hide();
    };
    $(window).resize(function () {
        if (isHomePage) {
            var nextwidth = $(window).width();
            if ((lastwidth >= $mobilehomepage) && (nextwidth < $mobilehomepage)) {
                hidehomepage();
            }
            else if ((lastwidth < $mobilehomepage) && (nextwidth >= $mobilehomepage)) {
                showhomepage();
            }
        }
        lastwidth = nextwidth;
    });

    var firstload = true;
    function animloadmore() {
        $(".lmpd1").css("color", $tgnorange);
        setTimeout(function () {
            $(".lmpd2").css("color", $tgnorange);
            setTimeout(function () {
                $(".lmpd3").css("color", $tgnorange);
                setTimeout(function () {
                    $(".loadMorePosts").hide();
                    $(".showMorePosts").show();
                    
                    $(".lmpd1").css("color", "#ffffff");
                    $(".lmpd2").css("color", "#ffffff");
                    $(".lmpd3").css("color", "#ffffff");
                }, 100);
            }, 100);
        }, 100);
    }

    function loadMorePosts() {
        var startnumber = '0';
        var lastArticleId = '';
        
 
 
        if (firstload) {
            //firstload = false;
        }
        else {
            startnumber = $(".article").length;
            pageId = $(".blogroll").attr("data-pageid");
            lastArticleId = $(".article").last().attr("data-id");
        }
        $.ajax({
            url: "/tgnservices/BlogRollService.asmx/GetMoreArticles?firstArticleId={BED21A32-A545-42FD-980A-CED1EED50710}&lastArticleId=" + lastArticleId + "&pageId=" + pageId + "&sidebarVersion=1",
            dataType: "json",
            type: "GET",
            /*
            data: {
                startNumber: startnumber,
                lastArticleId: lastArticleId,
                pageId: pageId
            },
            */
            success: function (data) {
                var source = $("#blogrollTemplate").html();
                var template = Handlebars.compile(source);
                var html = template(data);
                console.log(data);
                if (firstload) {
                    //$(".blogroll").after(html);
                    $(".thePosts").before(html);
                    $(".article").first().children("div.horizontalRule1").remove();
                    firstload = false;
                }
                else {
                    $(".article").last().after(html);
                    // If the height of the main content area had previously been adjusted with adjustHeight (on MasterLayout.aspx) it may need to be reset to its normal height
                    adjustHeight();
                }
                if (data.MoreArticles !== true) {
                    // ses remove LMP $(".loadMorePosts").toggle();
                }
                DisqusCommentsCounter();
                $(".bylinecomment").mouseenter(function () {
                    $(this).find(".bci").css("color", $tgnorange);
                });
                $(".bylinecomment").mouseleave(function () {
                    $(this).find(".bci").css("color", "#000000");
                });
                setTimeout(setCommentCounts, 3000);
                $("#postsDropdown").css("height", $(document).height());
                $(".dropdownContainer").css("height", $(document).height());
                //$(".gosocov").socoverlay();
                setgutter();
                expando(); // and expand the image if needed
                removeBlankImages();
                //articles = addArticleNumbers();
                var posquery = document.URL.indexOf("LastArticleId");
                if (posquery != -1) {
                    articleid = document.URL.substr(posquery + 14);
                    location.href = "#" + articleid;
                }
                bindOmnitureEvents();
            }
        });
    }
    function setCommentCounts() {
        $(".commentContainer").each(function (i, v) {
            getCommentCount(v);
        });
    }
    function getCommentCount (v) {
        var see = $(v).find(".disqusLink").text();
        if (see == "") {
           // setTimeout(getCommentCount(v), 3000);
            $(v).find(".commentCountBR").text("");
        }
        else {
            var i = parseInt(see);
            $(v).find(".commentCountBR").text(i.toString());
        }
    }

    function DisqusCommentsCounter() {
            /* * * DON'T EDIT BELOW THIS LINE * * */
            var s = document.createElement('script'); s.async = true;
            s.type = 'text/javascript';
            s.src = '//' + disqus_shortname + '.disqus.com/count.js';
            (document.getElementsByTagName('HEAD')[0] || document.getElementsByTagName('BODY')[0]).appendChild(s);
    }

    <script type="text/javascript">
        var iframeHeight = 0;
        $(document).ready(function () {
            $(".mainHolder").css("opacity", 1);
            $(".footerh").css("opacity", 1);

            //var iffh = $('iframe').contents().height();
            //console.log("height = " + iffh);
            $(".gutterscroll a").click(trackRelatedContent);
            //this.style.height = this.contentWindow.document.body.offsetHeight + 'px';
        });
        function trackRelatedContent() {
            try {
                var href = $(this).attr("href");
                s.events = 'event14';
                s.eVar11 = href;
                s.linkTrackVars = 'events,eVar11';
                s.linkTrackEvents = 'event14';
                s.tl(this, 'o', href);
            } catch (ex) {
                console.log(ex.message);
                console.log(ex.name);
            }
        }
        $('iframe').load(function () {
            //this.style.height =
            try {
                if ((this != null) && (this.contentWindow != null) && (this.contentWindow.document != null)) {
                    iframeHeight = this.contentWindow.document.body.offsetHeight + 'px';
                }
            }
            catch (error) {
             }
        });

        function resizeIframe(obj) {
            obj.style.height = obj.contentWindow.document.body.scrollHeight + 'px';
        }

        // adjusts height for bottom section to compensate for a full gutter
        function adjustHeight() {
            var gutterHeight = parseInt($("#gutterscroll").css("height"));
            //console.log("gutter height " + gutterHeight);
            var contentHeight = parseInt($("#mainContent").css("height"));
            if (contentHeight == 0) {
                contentHeight = parseInt($(".searchResults").css("height"));
            }
            //console.log("content height " + contentHeight);
            if (gutterHeight > contentHeight) {
                while ((gutterHeight > contentHeight) && ($(".gutterLong").children().length > 0)) {
                    $(".gutterLong").children().last().detach(); //css("display", "none");
                    gutterHeight = parseInt($("#gutterscroll").css("height"));
                    //console.log("new long gutter height " + gutterHeight);
                }
                if (gutterHeight == 0) {
                    $(".gutterShort").css("display", "block");
                    gutterHeight = parseInt($("#gutterscroll").css("height"));
                    //console.log("new short gutter height " + gutterHeight);
                }
                $("#guttercol").css("height", gutterHeight + "px");
            }
            var bottomHeight = parseInt($(".bottom").css("height"));
            /* take out until we are using iframes for content and then reverify that the quest pages are working
            if ($('#maincol, iframe').length) {
                var mifHeight = parseInt($("#maincol").css("height"));
                var iffh = $('iframe').contents().height();
                if (iffh != null) {
                    //if (iffh > mifHeight) {
                    $("#maincol").css("height", iffh + "px");
                    //}
                    $(".iframeHolder").css("display", "block");
                }
            }
            */
            if ($('.iframeHolder').length) {
                //var iffh = $('iframe').contents().height();
                //var iffhh = $('iframe').contentWindow.document.body.offsetHeight;
                $("#maincol").css("height", iframeHeight);
            }
            if (gutterHeight > contentHeight + bottomHeight) {
                bottomHeight = ((gutterHeight - contentHeight) + 20) + "px";
                $(".bottom .content").css("min-height", bottomHeight);
            }
            else {
                $(".bottom .content").css("min-height", "0");
            }
        }
    </script>
